# Riftbound Core Rules v1.2

> Converted from official PDF with structured rule layout.

<div class="rule-sheet">

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">Riftbound Core Rules</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">Last Updated: 2025-12-01</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-chapter level-0"><div class="rule-id">000.</div><div class="rule-text">Golden and Silver Rules</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">001.</div><div class="rule-text">Golden Rule</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">002.</div><div class="rule-text">Card text supersedes rules text. Whenever a card fundamentally contradicts the rules, the card&#x27;s indication is what is true.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">050.</div><div class="rule-text">Silver Rule</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">051.</div><div class="rule-text">Card text uses different terminology than rules. Card text should be interpreted according to these rules, not as though it were text within these rules.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">052.</div><div class="rule-text">Card , when written in card effects, is shorthand for &quot; Main Deck card.&quot; Runes, legends, and battlefields are not considered cards when executing the abilities and effects of game objects. They are considered cards for the purposes of these rules.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">053.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards refer to themselves in the first person.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">053.1.</div><div class="rule-text">* Units and legends say &quot;I,&quot; &quot;me,&quot; etc.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">053.2.</div><div class="rule-text">* Gear and spells say &quot;this.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">053.3.</div><div class="rule-text">* Battlefields say &quot;here.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">054.</div><div class="rule-text">&quot;Can&#x27;t beats Can&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">054.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards that forbid actions or effects, as a broad method of determination, supersede cards that allow or permit that same action or effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">055.</div><div class="rule-text">When executing card text, do as much as you can, ignoring impossible instructions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">055.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If all of a card&#x27;s instructions are impossible, it is still played and resolved, but nothing happens.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-chapter level-0"><div class="rule-id">100.</div><div class="rule-text">Game Concepts</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">101.</div><div class="rule-text">Deck Construction</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">102.</div><div class="rule-text">Riftbound is a Trading Card Game where a player must provide their own cards to play against other players.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">103.</div><div class="rule-text">To play Riftbound , a player must have two Decks, a Champion Legend , and a number of Battlefields determined by the Mode of Play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">103.1.</div><div class="rule-text">1 Champion Legend</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This is placed in the Legend Zone at the start of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This will dictate the Domain Identity of the Main Deck.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards included in your Deck must abide by your Domain Identity.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Your deck&#x27;s Domain Identity is dictated by the domains of your Champion Legend. In the default card frame, these domains appear as symbols in the legend&#x27;s upper left corner.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.1.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If a card has a single Domain , then that card is permitted in the Domain Identity that corresponds to the same Domain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.1.b.4.</div><div class="rule-text">If a card has more than one Domain , then that card is permitted only in a Domain Identity that contains all of the indicated Domains on that card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">103.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A Main Deck of at least 40 cards 1 Chosen Champion Unit Units Gear Spells</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Chosen Champion</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This will be placed in the Champion Zone at the start of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.2.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Must be a champion unit with a champion tag that matches the tag on your Champion Legend. Example: Loose Cannon has the tag Jinx . Therefore, a player could choose Jinx, Rebel or Jinx, Demolitionist as their Chosen Champion , because they also have the tag Jinx . Example: Tibbers has the tag Annie , but it is a signature unit, not a champion unit. It cannot be your Chosen Champion , even if your Champion Legend has the tag Annie .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.2.a.3.</div><div class="rule-text">A player&#x27;s Chosen Champion is both the specific card chosen for this slot during Deck Building and also any Champion Unit with the same name as the specific card selected for this specific slot during the course of play. Example: A player chose Jinx, Rebel as their Chosen Champion. One copy of Jinx, Rebel starts the game in their Chosen Champion zone. Any additional copies of Jinx, Rebel in their Main Deck, their hand, their trash, or on the board also count as their Chosen Champion for any game rules and effects that care about Chosen Champion status during the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Your Main Deck can include up to 3 copies of the same named card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This includes your Chosen Champion. Example: A deck could include Volibear, Furious as its Chosen Champion and still include 2 more copies of Volibear, Furious.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.2.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards have different names even if they represent the same character. Example: A deck could include 3 copies of Yasuo, Remorseful and 3 copies of Yasuo, Windrider, because they have different names.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Subject to Domain Identity.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.2.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Your deck may only contain 3 total Signature cards that have the same Champion tag as your Champion Legend.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.2.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Regardless of name, a deck may only contain a sum total of 3 Signature cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.2.d.2.</div><div class="rule-text">All of the Signature cards must have the Champion tag that corresponds to the Champion Legend of the deck.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.2.d.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Signature cards are not Champion units and cannot be placed in the Champion Zone .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.2.e.</div><div class="rule-text">During Gameplay, the Main Deck is Secret Information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.2.e.1.</div><div class="rule-text">It cannot be looked through or revealed unless instructed by a card effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">103.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Rune Deck</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">12 Rune Cards</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">103.3.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards in this deck must be of the Domain Identity of your Champion Legend.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Must be shuffled and kept separate from the Main Deck.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">103.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The number will be dictated by your Mode of Play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Subject to Domain Identity if applicable.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">103.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Cannot include more than one of a Battlefield of the same name when there are more than one required for the deck.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">104.</div><div class="rule-text">Setup</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">105.</div><div class="rule-text">Spaces</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">106.</div><div class="rule-text">The Play Area includes a space for Game Objects referred to as The Board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">106.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Board is divided into several Zones.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">106.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Base</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">One per player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The space each player always has access to play their Units and Gear to.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Base is a Location.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.2.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Other players cannot have Game Objects they control in another player&#x27;s Base.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.2.e.</div><div class="rule-text">The Base also houses each player&#x27;s Runes that are on The Board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">106.3.</div><div class="rule-text">The Battlefield Zone</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple Battlefields will be here, typically one per player, but occasionally less.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The space where Battlefields are located during gameplay.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Battlefield is individually a Location.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">106.4.</div><div class="rule-text">The Facedown Zones</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Battlefield is associated with a sub-zone called a Facedown Zone , a single logical space that a card can be put facedown in through various Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Facedown Zone has a maximum occupancy of one card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards can only be placed in or occupy the Facedown Zone if the controller of the card also controls the associated Battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.4.d.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Hidden card&#x27;s controller loses Control of the Battlefield , the card in the Facedown Zone is removed during the next Cleanup. See rule 318. Cleanups for more information. See rule 408. Hide for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.4.e.</div><div class="rule-text">Facedown Zones are not locations.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">106.5.</div><div class="rule-text">The Legend Zone</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The space for each player&#x27;s Champion Legend.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This is not a location.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.5.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The Champion Legend here is a Game Object. See rule 119. Game Objects for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">106.5.d.</div><div class="rule-text">The Champion Legend cannot be removed, moved, or displaced from this zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">107.</div><div class="rule-text">The Play Area also includes Non-Board Zones.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">107.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Trash</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This space is where cards are placed when they are killed or discarded, when they finish being executed as spells, when they are moved to the trash as an effect, etc.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Represents cards that have been used or spent.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player has a separate trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">A card owned by a player can never, for any reason, be put into a trash of another player. If it would be, it&#x27;s put into its owner&#x27;s trash instead.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.1.e.</div><div class="rule-text">The cards in the Trash are unordered. Their sequence does not matter, and they may be reorganized.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.1.f.</div><div class="rule-text">The cards in any player&#x27;s Trash are Public Information. See rule 127. Privacy for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">107.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Champion Zone</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The space each player puts their Chosen Champion at the start of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The Chosen Champion here cannot be returned to this zone by normal means.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">107.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Chosen Champion is instructed to be returned to this zone, it can only do so if there is not a card already in this zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The Chosen Champion can be played from here as normal, following the rules of Playing a Card. See rule 346. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">107.3.</div><div class="rule-text">The Main Deck Zone</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The space for the player&#x27;s Main Deck.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Primarily houses the face-down deck during gameplay.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The order of cards in the deck is Secret Information during the course of play. See rule 127. Privacy for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">107.4.</div><div class="rule-text">The Rune Deck Zone</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The space for the player&#x27;s Rune Deck.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Primarily houses the face-down runes during gameplay.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The order of runes in the deck is Secret Information during the course of play. See rule 127. Privacy for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">107.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Banishment</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This space is where cards are placed when they are banished by a spell or effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Represents cards that have been removed from play in a more difficult-to-recover way, or a temporary space to hold cards while effects are being processed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player has a separate banishment.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.d.</div><div class="rule-text">A card owned by a player can never, for any reason, be put into the banishment of another player. If it would be, it&#x27;s put into its owner&#x27;s banishment instead.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.e.</div><div class="rule-text">The cards in the banishment are unordered. Their sequence does not matter, and they may be reorganized.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.f.</div><div class="rule-text">The cards in any player&#x27;s Banishment are Public Information. See rule 127. Privacy for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.g.</div><div class="rule-text">Some spells or effects may reference cards placed into banishment directly.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.h.</div><div class="rule-text">Effects that reference cards in banishment only do so by means of also putting the cards there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.i.</div><div class="rule-text">The effects or references to cards in banishment do not count as Choosing.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.5.j.</div><div class="rule-text">The effects or references to cards in banishment do not count as Attachment.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">107.6.</div><div class="rule-text">The Hand</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player has a collection of cards they may Play cards from.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.6.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This is the location cards go when Drawn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.6.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The cards in a player&#x27;s hand are Private Information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.6.d.</div><div class="rule-text">The number of cards in a player&#x27;s hand is Public Information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.6.e.</div><div class="rule-text">The hand can be targeted as a zone, and cards there can be affected by spells and effects when specified.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">107.6.f.</div><div class="rule-text">A card owned by a player can never, for any reason, be put into the hand of another player. If it would be, it&#x27;s put into its owner&#x27;s hand instead.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">108.</div><div class="rule-text">All Game Objects in the collective Play Areas are Public Information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">108.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Any player may view, or be provided with the details of the face-up information printed on the cards in the Play Area.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">108.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The State of all Game Objects in the Play Area is also Public Information. Examples: If a Unit is Buffed If a Gear is Exhausted Etc.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">109.</div><div class="rule-text">Whenever a Game Object changes zones to or from a Non-Board Zone , all Temporary Modifications of all kinds cease to be tracked on it in all capacities. Examples: Damage is cleared. Buffs are removed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">Temporarily granted Keywords are no longer granted.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">110.</div><div class="rule-text">Setup Process</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">111.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player separates their Champion Legend and places it in the Legend Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">112.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player separates their Chosen Champion and places it in the Champion Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">113.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player sets aside their Battlefields.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">113.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Your Mode of Play will dictate how these are used and placed into the Battlefield Zone. See rule 458. Modes of Play for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">114.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player shuffles their decks, separately, then places them into their respective Zones.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">114.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Main Deck is placed in the Main Deck Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">114.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Rune Deck is placed in the Rune Deck Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">115.</div><div class="rule-text">Determine Turn Order using any fair random method agreed on by all players.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">115.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Turn Order is established as a repeating set of the players.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">115.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The Mode of Play will specify how to determine a First Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">115.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If not otherwise specified, Seating then determines the sequence, play proceeding clockwise from the First Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">115.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The First Player is the player who becomes the Turn Player first.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">115.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Turn Order repeats until the game ends.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">115.2.</div><div class="rule-text">See the selected Mode of Play for any adjustments to each player&#x27;s first turn. See rule 458. Modes of Play for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">116.</div><div class="rule-text">Players each draw 4.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">117.</div><div class="rule-text">In turn order, players perform their Mulligan.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">117.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A player may choose up to two cards in their hand. They set those cards aside.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">117.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Then, that player draws as many cards as they set aside.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">117.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Finally, that player Recycles the cards that were set aside. See rule 403. Recycle for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">118.</div><div class="rule-text">Begin play with the First Player taking their turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">119.</div><div class="rule-text">Game Objects</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">120.</div><div class="rule-text">A Game Object is any game piece that can produce one or more Game Effects or grant prerequisites for players to take Game Actions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">121.</div><div class="rule-text">A Game Object does not include nor preclude any inherent properties beyond the ability to produce, or act as the prerequisite for, Game Effects and Game Actions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">122.</div><div class="rule-text">A Game Object can be a literal object or a logical object.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">123.</div><div class="rule-text">Game Objects include, but are not limited to, the following: Main Deck cards in any zone Runes in any zone Legends</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields Tokens Abilities of any type on the chain Buffs and other status markers</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">124.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">125.</div><div class="rule-text">Riftbound games are composed of players playing the cards in their respective decks.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">126.</div><div class="rule-text">Ownership</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">126.1.</div><div class="rule-text">For gameplay purposes, a card&#x27;s Owner is the player who brought it into the game, either as their Champion Legend , one of their Battlefields , or part of their Main Deck or Rune Deck . The legal owner of a card doesn&#x27;t matter during gameplay. Example: Bo didn&#x27;t bring a deck, so Alice loans him a deck. During the game, Bo is considered the owner of those cards, even though legally they belong to Alice.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">127.</div><div class="rule-text">Privacy</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">127.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A card will always exist in one of the many Zones described during Setup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">127.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A card will have a different level of Privacy based on where it resides at a given time</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">127.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Secret: This level of Privacy indicates that neither player may read or look at the face of the card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">127.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Private: This level of Privacy indicates that only the controller of a card on the board or the owner of a card in any other zone may read or look at the face of the card. Example: Cards in a player&#x27;s hand are owned by that player. Only that player may read or look at their faces. Example: If a player controls a facedown card at a battlefield, that player and only that player may read or look at that card&#x27;s face, regardless of who owns that card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">127.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Public: This level of Privacy indicates that any player may read or look at the face of the card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">128.</div><div class="rule-text">Back Side</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">128.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The back side of a card is the side with the Riftbound logo.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">128.2.</div><div class="rule-text">There is a unique pattern of back side for each of the three categories of card: Main Deck cards, Rune Deck cards, and Battlefields and Champion Legends.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">128.3.</div><div class="rule-text">The back side of a card is presented to conceal information for Private and Secret information cards. For example, cards in the Main Deck and cards in hand have their back side presented.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">128.4.</div><div class="rule-text">The term facedown is used to describe the state during regular play of having a card&#x27;s back side presented on the Board. A facedown card&#x27;s front side is considered Private Information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">129.</div><div class="rule-text">Front Side</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">129.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The front side of a card is the opposite of its back.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">129.2.</div><div class="rule-text">This is also referred to as a front face.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">129.3.</div><div class="rule-text">This can be identified in situations where the back is not easily discernible by the presence of the Play Cost in the upper left corner of the card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">129.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards, when played, are played with their front face presented.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">129.5.</div><div class="rule-text">The term face up is used to describe the state during regular play of having a card&#x27;s front face presented</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">129.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards are considered to be Public Information while in this state, even if obscured by other cards in a pile. Example: The Trash is Public Information because all cards there have their front face presented even while stacked.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">130.</div><div class="rule-text">Cost</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">130.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Main Deck cards have a Cost , listed in the upper left corner of the front face of the card. See rule 161. Rune Pools for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">130.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Energy Cost</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">130.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The numeral listed in the Cost element in the upper left corner of the card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">130.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Power cost</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">130.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The symbols, listed vertically, in the Cost element in the upper left corner of the card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">130.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This section may not be present on every card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">130.</div><div class="rule-text">4 Effects that need to determine a card&#x27;s cost for any purpose always use its base cost, even if that cost is altered or ignored as the card is played. Example: Sky Splitter is a spell that costs 8 Energy and says in part &quot;This spell&#x27;s Energy cost is reduced by the highest Might among units you control.&quot; Lux, Illuminated is a unit that says &quot;When you play a spell that costs 5 or more, give me +3 [M] this turn.&quot; If a player who controls Lux plays Sky Splitter, Lux&#x27;s ability will trigger, regardless of how much was actually paid for Sky Splitter.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">131.</div><div class="rule-text">Name</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">131.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Each card has a name that identifies it uniquely.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">131.2.</div><div class="rule-text">This is usually located in the middle of the card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">131.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards that are printed in different languages but represent the same card are considered to have the same name for the purposes of deckbuilding and gameplay. Example: Chemtech Enforcer in English and its counterpart in Chinese are considered the same card, despite the Name element on the card reading differently.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">131.</div><div class="rule-text">4 Some cards have both a short name and a subtitle. For all purposes, including rules and deckbuilding, such a card&#x27;s name is &quot;[Short Name], [Subtitle]&quot;. Example: Kai&#x27;Sa, Evolutionary and Kai&#x27;Sa, Survivor both have the short name Kai&#x27;Sa, but they have different names. You can include 3 of each in your deck under normal deckbuilding rules. If one of them is your Chosen Champion, the other is not.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">132.</div><div class="rule-text">Category</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">132.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A card can have one or more Categories and Sub-Categories based on the properties of its front and back sides.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">132.2.</div><div class="rule-text">These Categories and Sub-Categories dictate the behaviors of the card during play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">132.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Spells and other effects can refer to categories, sub-categories, supertypes, card types, tags, and other characteristics inclusively or exclusively. Example: A &quot;non-unit card&quot; is any card that is not a unit. Example: A &quot;unit&quot; is any game object that is a unit, regardless of any other categories it belongs to.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">132.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Main Deck Cards begin the game in the Main Deck or (in the case of a Chosen Champion ) the Champion Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Permanents</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">132.4.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">An umbrella sub-category encompassing Main Deck Game Objects that remain on the board after being played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">132.4.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Unit and Gear are permanent types.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Spells</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">132.4.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A sub-category encompassing Main Deck cards with the spell type, which do not remain on the board after being played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">132.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Rune Deck Cards begin the game in the Rune Deck.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Runes</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">132.5.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A sub-category encompassing cards with the rune type. These are channeled rather than played. They remain on the board after being channeled, but they are not permanents, as they are not Main Deck cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">132.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Non-Deck Cards are not part of any deck and begin the game in a zone determined by their type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">132.6.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A sub-category encompassing cards with the battlefield type. They are not played or channeled. They start the game on the board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.6.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">132.6.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A sub-category encompassing cards with the legend type. They are not played or channeled. They start the game in the Legend Zone and cannot leave it during play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">132.7.</div><div class="rule-text">Supertypes are Categories that may apply to game objects of multiple types. They are listed before a card&#x27;s type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.7.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Champion is a supertype that applies exclusively to units. It impacts the rules for deckbuilding. See rule 103.2.a. Chosen Champion for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.7.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Signature is a supertype that may apply to game objects of any card type. It impacts the rules for deckbuilding. See rule 103.2.d. for more information about Signature cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.7.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Token is a supertype applied to temporary game objects of any card type. See rule 173. Tokens for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">132.8.</div><div class="rule-text">Tags are Categories that may apply to game objects of multiple types. They are listed after a card&#x27;s type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.8.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Tags have no innate rules meaning, but may be referenced by game rules and card effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">132.8.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Tags used to link Legends , Champion Units , and Signature cards are known as Champion Tags.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">133.</div><div class="rule-text">Domain</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">133.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Most cards belong to one or more of six Domains , identified by one or more symbols in the lower right corner.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">133.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Domain has an associated color, a unique symbol, and a shorthand used to represent that symbol in written text.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">133.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Fury is associated with the color red and represented by a circular symbol with three projecting points. Its shorthand is [R].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">133.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Calm is associated with the color green and represented by a symbol resembling a leaf. Its shorthand is [G].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">133.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Mind is associated with the color blue and represented by a symbol resembling a sun and moon. Its shorthand is [B].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">133.2.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Body is associated with the color orange and represented by a blocky diamond-shaped symbol. Its shorthand is [O].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">133.2.e.</div><div class="rule-text">Chaos is associated with the color purple and represented by a hexagonal symbol with swirls emanating from its center. Its shorthand is [P].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">133.2.f.</div><div class="rule-text">Order is associated with the color yellow and represented by an angular winged symbol. Its shorthand is [Y].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">134.</div><div class="rule-text">Rules Text</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">134.1.</div><div class="rule-text">All cards have a section that describes how they affect the game. This section is known as the Rules Text of the card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">134.2.</div><div class="rule-text">This section may contain:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">134.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Abilities</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Abilities are discrete pieces of text that describe what a card may or must do. See rule 357. Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">They may appear on any card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">134.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Instructions</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Instructions are a type of text that appears on spells and within abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">They describe the actions to be taken as the spell or ability resolves.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">134.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Keywords</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Keywords are short words or phrases that represent longer abilities or instructions. See rule 726. Keywords for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Keywords may or may not have reminder text.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">134.2.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Reminder Text</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Reminder text appears in italics and parentheses.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.d.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Its purpose is to summarize relevant rules, including keywords and other rules.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.d.3.</div><div class="rule-text">The presence, absence, or exact wording of reminder text has no effect on game function.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.</div><div class="rule-text">Symbols</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Rules text sometimes contains symbols that express game concepts. Each symbol also has a shorthand used to represent it in written text.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The cost of Exhausting a Permanent is represented by the &quot;exhaust symbol,&quot; which resembles a card turning sideways. Its shorthand is [E]. (Some previous rules information has given its shorthand as [T].)</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Might is represented by the &quot;Might symbol,&quot; which resembles a sword and shield. Its shorthand is [M]. (Some previous rules information has given its shorthand as [S].)</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Power of a specific Domain is represented by its domain symbol and the corresponding shorthand. See rule 133. Domain for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Power of any Domain is represented by a swirling rainbow symbol. Its shorthand is [A].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">When required as a cost, [A] can be paid by Power of any Domain .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">When Added to a player&#x27;s Rune Pool, [A] can be spent to pay a Power cost of any Domain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Power of a domain corresponding to a card&#x27;s own Domain is not represented by a symbol, but appears in these rules similarly to other symbols. Its shorthand is [C].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">When a [C] shorthand is printed on a card as reminder text, it assumes that card&#x27;s usual Domain , but it still means &quot;one Power of this card&#x27;s Domain .&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">134.2.e.6.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A [C] shorthand on a card with no Domain or with multiple Domains is processed as [A] instead.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">134.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Rules text can be blank.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">134.4.</div><div class="rule-text">A card&#x27;s Rules Text is Inactive while that card is Attached to another card. See rule 716 Attachment for more information. See rule 720 Inactive for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">134.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The presence of text, rules, Keywords , and other effects can still be referenced and detected by other game effects, even while Rules Text is Inactive.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">135.</div><div class="rule-text">Effect Text</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">135.</div><div class="rule-text">1 Some cards have a separate section of text below the Rules Text . This is referred to as the Effect Text .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">135.</div><div class="rule-text">2 Effect Text can contain additional Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">135.2.</div><div class="rule-text">a Effect Text can be blank.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">135.2.</div><div class="rule-text">b Effect Text is inactive unless the card with the Effect Text is Attached to another card. See rule 716 Attachment for more information. See rule 720 Inactive for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">135.2.</div><div class="rule-text">c The abilities in the Effect Text section of a card are appended to the Rules Text of the card to which the card with the Effect Text is Attached.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">136.</div><div class="rule-text">Might Bonus</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">136.</div><div class="rule-text">1 Some cards have a Might Bonus in their lower right corner, expressed as an operator plus an integer.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">136.</div><div class="rule-text">2 A card&#x27;s Might Bonus can be +0.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">136.</div><div class="rule-text">3 A card&#x27;s Might Bonus modulates the Might of the card to which the card that has the Might Bonus is Attached . See rule 716 Attachment for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">136.3.</div><div class="rule-text">a The Might Bonus is applied while Attached and stops applying as soon as the card with the Might Bonus is no longer Attached.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">136.3.</div><div class="rule-text">b If the card to which a card with a Might Bonus is Attached has no Might value, the Might Bonus is ignored.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">137.</div><div class="rule-text">Flavor Text</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">137.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Flavor text is text that appears at the bottom of some cards to provide aesthetic enjoyment. It conveys no gameplay information. Example: The card Void Seeker features a quote from the character Kai&#x27;Sa. It does not have the Kai&#x27;Sa tag and has no gameplay connection to the Champion unit Kai&#x27;Sa.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">137.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Flavor text is located at the bottom of the section provided for rules text, usually in a shaded bar. It appears in italics.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">138.</div><div class="rule-text">Illustration</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">138.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Each card has an illustration. It conveys no gameplay information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">139.</div><div class="rule-text">Units</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">140.</div><div class="rule-text">Unit is :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">140.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A Game Object</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">140.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">While on the Board :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">140.1.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Units are at one of several Locations while on the Board : a Battlefield or their Base.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">140.1.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Units and their details are Public Information while on the Board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">140.1.a.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Units can be chosen, affected, or manipulated by spells, affects, or game actions that specify Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">140.1.a.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Units can be Killed. See rule 415. Kill for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">140.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">While in the Trash:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">140.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Units are treated as Cards , similar to when in the Hand.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">140.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">They retain the properties of being a Unit , but are not on the Board and thus cannot take actions or be affected by spells, abilities, or game actions that target Units on the Board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">140.1.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Units can be affected by spells and game effects that target Units in the Trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">140.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A Card Type</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">140.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This is a unique identifier that some spells or abilities will use to restrict what they can choose or affect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">140.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The card type is relevant in all zones.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">141.</div><div class="rule-text">Damage is a marked value that is applied to Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">141.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Damage is not a Game Object.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">141.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Damage is a value tracked per-Unit.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">141.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Damage tracks how close a Unit is to being Killed. See rule 415. Kill for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">141.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Damage can be Healed. See rule 405. Heal for more information .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">142.</div><div class="rule-text">Units have multiple Intrinsic Properties unique to them:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">142.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Tag: A Unit has zero or more Tags representing one or more champions, regions, factions, or species it belongs to.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">142.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">These have no intrinsic rules or behaviors by themselves.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">142.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Spells, abilities, and game actions can reference these types as part of their execution.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">142.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Might : The combat statistic of a Unit . Used to determine a Unit&#x27;s contribution to Combat , as well as when it is Killed by damaging effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">142.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Unit ever has nonzero damage marked on it equalling or exceeding its Might , it is Killed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">142.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If a unit&#x27;s Might is ever less than 0, it is treated as 0 for all purposes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">142.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Units can have damage marked on them.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">142.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">When spells, abilities, or other game effects deal damage, Units mark that damage on them temporarily. This can be tracked with coins, dice, or other markers, or by memory.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">142.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Damage is Healed from Units at two specific times:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">142.3.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">At the end of each player&#x27;s turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">142.3.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">During a Combat Cleanup. See rule 444.1. for more information about Combat Cleanups.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">142.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Units enter the Board exhausted.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">142.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This can be altered by Accelerate or similar game effects. See rule 731. Accelerate for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">143.</div><div class="rule-text">Units have the Inherent Ability to perform a Standard Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">143.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This action is limited in when it can be performed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">143.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This action can be done any time during a player&#x27;s Action Phase.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">143.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This action cannot be performed during a Closed State .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">143.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">This action cannot be performed during a Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">143.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Exhausting the Unit is the Cost for this action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">143.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Players may perform multiple Units&#x27; standard move simultaneously.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">143.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Move like this is declared by a player, the units&#x27; Destination must be the same.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">143.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Move like this is declared by a player, the Origins do not need to be the same.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">143.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The Costs of Exhausting the Units are also paid Simultaneously.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">143.4.</div><div class="rule-text">The Destinations where Units can Move to with their Standard Move are restricted:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">143.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Units may move from their Base to a Battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">143.4.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Units cannot Move to a Battlefield that already has units from 2 other players present.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">143.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Units may move from a Battlefield to their Base.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">143.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Ganking is a unique ability that affects a Unit&#x27;s Standard Move</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">143.4.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Units with Ganking may use their Standard Move to Move from Battlefield to Battlefield. See rule 736. Ganking for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">144.</div><div class="rule-text">Units may have Activated Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">144.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Activated Abilities are Game Effects that are written as Costs followed by a &quot;:&quot;, and then succeeded by an effect. See rule 369. Activated Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">144.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Activated Ability of Units may be executed at any time during the controlling player&#x27;s Action Phase during an Open State , and not during a Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">144.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This follows the same process as playing a card. See rule 346. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">144.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This behaves, once activated, like a spell without an associated card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">145.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">146.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear are:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">146.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A Game Object</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">146.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">While on the Board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">146.1.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear can only be played to a player&#x27;s Base.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">146.1.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear and their details are Public Information while on the Board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">146.1.a.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear can be chosen, affected, or manipulated by spells, effects, or game actions that specify Gear.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">146.1.a.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear can be Killed. See rule 415. Kill for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">146.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">While in the Trash</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">146.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear are treated as Cards before Game Objects , similar to the Hand.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">146.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">They retain the properties of being Gear , but are not on the Board and thus cannot take actions or be affected by spells, abilities, or game actions that affect Gear on the Board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">146.1.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear can be affected by spells and game effects that affect Gear in the Trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">146.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A Card Type</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">146.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This is a unique identifier that some spells or abilities will use to restrict what they can choose or affect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">146.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The card type is relevant in all zones.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">147.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear have several Intrinsic Properties unique to them.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">147.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear enters play Ready.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">147.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear can only be played to a player&#x27;s Base.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">147.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Gear is at a Battlefield for any reason, then it is immediately recalled to its controller&#x27;s Base as a corrective action. See rule 432. Recalls for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">148.</div><div class="rule-text">Gear may have Activated Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">148.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Activated Abilities are Game Effects that are written as Costs followed by a &quot;:&quot;, and then succeeded by an effect. See rule 369. Activated Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">148.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Activated Ability of Gear may be executed at any time during the controlling player&#x27;s Action Phase during an Open State , and not during a Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">148.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This follows the same process as playing a card. See rule 346. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">148.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This behaves, once activated, like a spell without an associated card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">149.</div><div class="rule-text">Spells</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">150.</div><div class="rule-text">Spell is a card type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">151.</div><div class="rule-text">A spell can be played during an Open State Outside of Showdowns on its controller&#x27;s turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">152.</div><div class="rule-text">A spell is controlled by the player who played it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">153.</div><div class="rule-text">A spell creates a game effect according to its instructions and is then placed in the Trash of the player who owns it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">154.</div><div class="rule-text">When a spell is successfully played, a player executes the rules text of the spell. This is called Resolving the spell.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">154.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Spells have their rules text executed from top to bottom when they are Resolved.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">154.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If a later part of a spell applies a Replacement Effect that alters earlier parts of the spell, apply those replacement effects as appropriate. Example: A spell says &quot;Choose a unit. Kill it the next time it takes damage this turn.&quot; and &quot;[Legion] - Kill it now instead. (Get the effect if you&#x27;ve played another card this turn.) &quot; If the Legion condition is satisfied, the unit is killed immediately and the instruction to kill it the next time it takes damage is ignored, even if the unit remains on the board somehow.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">154.3.</div><div class="rule-text">While a spell or ability on the chain is Resolving , no other spells or abilities can be finalized on the chain or resolved, including triggered abilities or game effects that would occur as a result of the execution of the spell.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">154.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Finish resolving all effects of a spell before addressing anything the spell may have triggered or caused through execution.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">155.</div><div class="rule-text">Certain Keywords on spells are not executable rules text, but instead intrinsic properties of the spell.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">155.1.</div><div class="rule-text">These determine inherent properties and behaviors of the spell before being played or while on the chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">155.2.</div><div class="rule-text">These keywords are:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">155.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Action</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">155.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This indicates that, in addition to being able to be played during an Open State , this spell may also be played during Open States during Showdowns.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">155.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Reaction</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">155.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Grants all cases and rules of Action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">155.2.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">In addition to all prior cases, may also be played during all forms of Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">155.2.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">This will result in this spell resolving before spells and abilities that are already on the chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">156.</div><div class="rule-text">Runes</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">157.</div><div class="rule-text">Rune is a Card Type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">157.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A Rune is not a Main Deck card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">157.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This means, despite remaining on the Board until Recycled or otherwise removed from the board, it is not a Permanent.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">157.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Runes are kept in the Rune Deck.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">157.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Exactly 12 Rune cards chosen during Deck Construction. See rule 103.3. Rune Deck for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">157.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Rune is Recycled it is returned to the Rune Deck , not the Main Deck. See rule 403. Recycle for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">158.</div><div class="rule-text">Runes produce the resources needed to pay costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">159.</div><div class="rule-text">Runes produce Energy and Power.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">159.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Energy is used to pay numeric Energy costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">159.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Energy has no Domain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">159.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Energy has no type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">159.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Power is used to pay Domain-associated Power Costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">159.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Power has a Domain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">159.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Power &#x27;s Domain usually corresponds to the Domain of the Rune that produced it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">159.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Some Power is Universal and can be used to pay for costs of any Domain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">160.</div><div class="rule-text">Basic Runes</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">160.1.</div><div class="rule-text">There are six Basic Runes , each with a Domain corresponding to its name: Fury Rune Calm Rune Mind Rune Body Rune Chaos Rune Order Rune</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">160.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A Basic Rune always has the following two Abilities :</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">160.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">[E]: [Reaction] - Add [1].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">160.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Recycle this: [Reaction] - Add [C].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">160.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Power added this way corresponds to the Domain of the Rune that is being Recycled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">161.</div><div class="rule-text">Rune Pools</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">162.</div><div class="rule-text">The Rune Pool is a conceptual collection of a player&#x27;s available Energy and Power available to pay Costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">162.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When a card adds Energy or Power, it is added to the controlling player&#x27;s Rune Pool .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">162.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Players must first add Energy and Power to their Rune Pool in order to be able to spend it to play cards or pay for Abilities with costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">162.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Energy and Power do not have a physical marker or tracker, although players may wish to use a physical tracker if they are retaining unspent Energy and Power over the course of their turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">163.</div><div class="rule-text">Every player&#x27;s Rune Pool empties at the end of each player&#x27;s draw phase and the end of each player&#x27;s turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">163.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Any unspent Energy or Power are lost.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">164.</div><div class="rule-text">All Abilities that include the action &quot; Add &quot; are abilities that are adding Energy or Power to the Rune Pool. See rule 416. Add for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">165.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">166.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are Game Objects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are Owned by a player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are not shuffled into Decks at the start of a game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">166.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are not played during the course of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">166.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are established at the start of a game and remain in place for the duration of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields cannot be Killed during the course of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields cannot be Moved.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are Locations.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">166.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be Origins of moves.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">166.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be Destinations of moves.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Any number of Units can be present at a Battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.7.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can be targeted by spells or game effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.8.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can have Passive Abilities. See rule 360. Passive Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">166.9.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields can have Triggered Abilities. See rule 375. Triggered Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">167.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields are not Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">168.</div><div class="rule-text">The number of Battlefields on the Board is determined by the Mode of Play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">169.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends</div></div>
