<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">170.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are Game Objects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">170.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are Owned by a player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">170.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are not shuffled into Decks at the start of a game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">170.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are not played during the course of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">170.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are established at the start of a game, and remain in place for the duration of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">170.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends cannot be Killed during the course of regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">170.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends cannot be Moved.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">170.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends can be targeted by spells or game effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">170.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends can have Passive Abilities. See rule 360. Passive Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">170.7.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends can have Triggered Abilities. See rule 375. Triggered Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">170.8.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends can have Activated Abilities. See rule 369. Activated Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">171.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends are not Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">172.</div><div class="rule-text">Legends may have one or more Domains.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">172.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Legend determines the Domain Identity of cards its owner can include. See rule 101. Deck Construction for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">173.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">174.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are Game Objects created by spells and abilities during play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">175.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens can be represented by anything. Printed tokens are included in Riftbound booster packs, but they are not required to play a token.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">176.</div><div class="rule-text">A token&#x27;s controller is the controller of the spell or ability that created it, unless the token&#x27;s type innately determines control or that spell or ability specifies that a different player is the token&#x27;s controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">177.</div><div class="rule-text">A token&#x27;s owner is the player who controlled the effect that created it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">178.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect that creates a token may specify the conditions or circumstances under which it enters the board. These stipulations may alter the usual steps for playing a card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">178.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect may state that the token enters ready or exhausted, if that state is contrary to the default for the token&#x27;s type.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">178.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect may restrict the location to which the token may be played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">178.3.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect may grant temporary abilities or modifications to the token.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">179.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are not cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">179.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens have some properties in common with cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">179.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are played by their owner if their card type is played, following all the applicable steps for playing a card plus any restrictions or modifications from the effect that created the token. See rule 346. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">179.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Token units have a Might .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">179.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens may have one or more tags .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">179.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens have a type . They follow all rules for their type unless otherwise specified. Example: A token unit is a unit. It enters exhausted, can take the standard move action, deals damage equal to its Might in combat, is destroyed if it takes damage equal to or greater than its might, can be chosen or otherwise affected by spells or abilities that choose or affect units, etc.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">179.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens differ from cards in some ways.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">179.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens do not have costs .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">179.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens do not have domains .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">180.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are created on the board and cannot exist elsewhere.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">180.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If a token is put into any Non-Board Zone , it ceases to exist immediately after moving to its new zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">181.</div><div class="rule-text">The spell or ability that creates a token specifies some of its characteristics. It may have other characteristics, as listed below.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">181.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A 1[M] Recruit token is a domainless unit token with 1 Might and the Recruit tag.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">181.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A 3[M] Sprite token with Temporary is a domainless unit token with 3 Might, the Fae tag, and the Temporary keyword. See rule 742. Temporary for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">182.</div><div class="rule-text">Control</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">183.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is the concept of a player having influence of a Game Object and applies differently to different card types.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">184.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is established over Battlefields through the course of play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is a binary state for Battlefields and an Identifier for players.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A Battlefield is Controlled or Uncontrolled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A Battlefield is Controlled by a specific player or Controlled by no one.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Control can be Contested through the course of play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Contested is a temporary status applied to the battlefield when a Unit controlled by a Player who does not currently Control that Battlefield Moves or otherwise becomes present there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">184.3.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Units moving to or being played to a battlefield apply Contested status if that battlefield is not already contested and that Unit &#x27;s controller does not already control that battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A Battlefield remains Contested until Control is established or re-established.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">While a Battlefield remains Contested, Control of a Battlefield cannot change.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.3.d.</div><div class="rule-text">The state of a Battlefield being Contested is used to determine when Combat should occur, when a Showdown without a Combat should occur, and when Control will change.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.3.e.</div><div class="rule-text">At this time Game Effects cannot reference this status.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is established by having Units at a Battlefield at the end of a Showdown or Combat after applying the contested status.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If a player controls Units at a Battlefield, outside of Combat , they maintain Control of that Battlefield for as long as they have Units at that Battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A player maintains control of a Battlefield while it is being Contested by an opponent.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">If a player has no Units at a Battlefield, they lose Control of that Battlefield immediately, unless it is Contested.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is a constant state.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">184.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Control of a Battlefield determines Control of its Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">While a Battlefield is Controlled , its Controller controls its Abilities . That player takes responsibility for adding them to the Chain if applicable, and makes all choices required by them unless otherwise specified.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.6.b.</div><div class="rule-text">While a Battlefield is Uncontrolled , its Abilities are also Uncontrolled. The Turn Player takes responsibility for adding them to the Chain if applicable, makes all choices required by them unless otherwise specified, and is treated as their Controller if any game rule or effect requires one. Example: The Arena&#x27;s Greatest is a battlefield that reads &quot;At the start of each player&#x27;s first Beginning Phase, that player gains 1 point.&quot; This ability will usually trigger while the battlefield has no controller. If it does, the Turn Player goes through the steps of adding the ability to the chain and receives priority after doing so, exactly as if they controlled the ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">184.6.c.</div><div class="rule-text">&quot;You&quot; in a battlefield&#x27;s abilities refers to the battlefield&#x27;s Controller , as does the implied &quot;you&quot; in instructions like &quot;draw 1.&quot; If the battlefield has no Controller , &quot;you&quot; refers to no one, and all such instructions are ignored.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">185.</div><div class="rule-text">Everything Else</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">185.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When a player Plays a Card or other Game Object , they are established as that Game Object&#x27;s Controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">185.2.</div><div class="rule-text">For Spells , they are the Spell&#x27;s Controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">That player chooses targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">That player chooses modes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">That player pays costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">185.3.</div><div class="rule-text">For Permanents and Runes , when they Enter the Board , that player is assigned as that Game Object&#x27;s Controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">That player may make decisions about the Game Object&#x27;s Inherent Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">That player may make decisions about the Game Object&#x27;s Unique Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">That player may make decisions about any game effects or decisions necessary while the card is being played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.3.d.</div><div class="rule-text">That player may make decisions about any game effects created from &quot;When you play me&quot; effects of Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">185.4.</div><div class="rule-text">For Abilities , they are the Ability&#x27;s Controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">By default, the Controller of an Ability&#x27;s Source is the Controller of that Ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Changes to Control of an Ability&#x27;s Source do not change Control of that Ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">That player chooses targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.4.d.</div><div class="rule-text">That player chooses modes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">185.4.e.</div><div class="rule-text">That player pays costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">186.</div><div class="rule-text">When a game effect or rules text refers to the Controller of a specific object, it can be referring to either context interchangeably.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">186.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The method of assignment of control is different, but the status of Control is the same across all Game Objects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-chapter level-0"><div class="rule-id">300.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing the Game</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">301.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">302.</div><div class="rule-text">Play continues cyclically until one player wins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">303.</div><div class="rule-text">The phases of a turn are rigid, but the actions taken during those steps can be done in any order, unless otherwise specified.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">303.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Game Actions of any nature are performed one at a time and are executed completely.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">303.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Game Actions cannot be performed simultaneously for any reason.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">303.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If one or more actions, game effects, or Triggered Abilities are activated simultaneously, then Turn Order is referenced to organize the sequence of actions. See rule 375. Triggered Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">304.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player is the player taking the current turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">305.</div><div class="rule-text">When there are no items on the Chain and the Turn Player cannot or chooses not to perform any Discretionary Actions , the current phase or step of the turn ends and the next phase, step, or turn begins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">306.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player changes when the current Turn Player reaches the End of all of the Phases of their Turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">307.</div><div class="rule-text">States of the Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">308.</div><div class="rule-text">At any given time, the turn is in either a Neutral State or a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">308.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Showdown is in progress, the turn is in a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">308.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Only cards and abilities with the Action or Reaction keywords can be played or activated in a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">308.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If no Showdown is in progress, the turn is in a Neutral State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">309.</div><div class="rule-text">At any given time, the turn is in either an Open State or a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">309.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Chain exists, the turn is in a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">309.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Only cards and abilities with the Reaction keyword can be played or activated in a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">309.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If no Chain exists, the turn is in an Open State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">310.</div><div class="rule-text">These descriptions can be combined, such that the turn is always in one of these four states:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">310.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Neutral Open: There is no Showdown in progress and no Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">310.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">By default, cards can be played and abilities activated only when a player has priority on their turn in a Neutral Open state.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">310.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Neutral Closed: There is no Showdown in progress and a Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">310.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdown Open: A Showdown is in progress and no Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">310.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdown Closed: A Showdown is in progress and a Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">311.</div><div class="rule-text">Priority and Focus</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">312.</div><div class="rule-text">At any given time, up to one player has Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">312.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Priority is the singular exclusive right to take Discretionary Actions. See rule 398.1. Discretionary Actions for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The player with Priority can take appropriately timed Discretionary Actions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If no player has Priority , no player can take Discretionary Actions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">312.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Players can always take and make choices for Limited Actions when instructed, regardless of Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">312.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A player receives Priority at the following times:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">When the turn is in a Neutral Open State during their Action Phase.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">When the turn is in a Showdown State and they gain Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">When the turn is in a Closed State and they control the next item on the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">312.2.d.</div><div class="rule-text">When the turn is in a Closed State , they are the next Player in Turn Order , and the player with Priority passes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">312.</div><div class="rule-text">3 When a player is granted Priority, it is either created if no player has it or taken from the player with Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">313.</div><div class="rule-text">At any given time, up to one player has Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">313.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Focus is the permission to take appropriately timed Discretionary Actions when the turn is in a Showdown Open State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">See rule 307. States of the Turn for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">313.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The player with Focus must obey any additional restrictions on which Discretionary Actions may be performed. Example: A player with Focus may not play spells or activate abilities that don&#x27;t have the Action or Reaction keywords.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">313.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A player who gains Focus also gains Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">313.3.</div><div class="rule-text">A player who passes Priority retains Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">313.</div><div class="rule-text">4 A player may not make discretionary actions with Focus unless they also possess Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">313.5.</div><div class="rule-text">If the turn is in a Neutral State , no player has Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">314.</div><div class="rule-text">Phases of the Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">315.</div><div class="rule-text">Start of Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">315.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Awaken Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player readies all Game Objects they control that are able to be readied. See rule 402. Ready for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">315.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Beginning Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Beginning Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">At the start of Beginning Phase game effects take place.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Scoring Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Holding occurs at this time. See rule 445. Scoring for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.2.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Reminder: In Modes of Play with Teams , Battlefields held by a Teammate of the Turn Player during this phase are disqualified from being scored this turn by the Turn Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Specific game effects or abilities will reference this timing and phase as necessary.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">315.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Channel Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player gains their additional runes for the turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player channels 2 runes from their Rune Deck. See rule 417. Channel for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.3.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are fewer than 2 runes in the Rune Deck, they channel as many as possible.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Perform any actions as instructed by game objects during this time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">315.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Draw Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player gains their additional card for the turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player draws 1.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.4.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are no cards remaining in their Main Deck to draw, the Turn Player has been Burned Out . See rule 418. Burn Out for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">315.4.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">After completing the Burn Out the Turn Player still Draws 1.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Perform any actions as instructed by game objects during this time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">315.4.d.</div><div class="rule-text">As the Draw Phase ends, each player&#x27;s Rune Pool empties. See rule 161. Rune Pools for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">316.</div><div class="rule-text">Action Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When all steps of the Start of Turn have been completed, the Action Phase begins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Action Phase has no defined structure.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A player may take any number of Discretionary Actions they are able to perform during this phase. See rule 398.1. Discretionary Actions for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This is denoted as a Neutral Open State , and only the Turn Player has the ability to play spells or activate abilities. See rule 307. States of the Turn for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">316.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">In Modes of Play with teammates, the Turn Player&#x27;s teammates may play spells and activate abilities, including ones without Action or Reaction.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">In Modes of Play with Teammates, spells may be played by Teammates of the Turn Player during this time, but the actions of the Turn Player take precedence.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.3.</div><div class="rule-text">As a result of a player taking Discretionary Actions , one or more structured phases may occur.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Combat</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A Combat phase occurs as a result of Units controlled by opposing players being present at the same Battlefield .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This could be the result of a Standard Move Standard Action , a Spell , or other Game Effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The source effect does not change the structure or flow of Combat once initiated.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.d.</div><div class="rule-text">A Combat can only occur between two players. See rule 437. Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.e.</div><div class="rule-text">Play proceeds following the steps of combat. See rule 441. Steps of Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.4.f.</div><div class="rule-text">Combat will also include a Showdown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdowns</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown occurs when a Combat occurs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">316.5.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdowns that occur as a result of Combat are a Sub-Phase of Combat.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown is marked as Staged at a Battlefield when the Contested status is applied to a Battlefield with no current controller.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">316.5.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdowns that occur as a result of a player moving to an empty Battlefield are a stand-alone Phase and do not create a Combat.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.5.c.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown is a structured Window of Opportunity where Players may play cards and activate abilities with Action or Reaction. See rule 337. Showdowns for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">316.6.</div><div class="rule-text">When a player has no more Discretionary Actions they wish to execute, they must indicate they are ending their turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This ends the Action Phase.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">316.6.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Play proceeds to the End of Turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">317.</div><div class="rule-text">End of Turn Phase</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">317.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Ending Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">At the end of the turn Game Effects take place.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Specific game effects and abilities will reference this timing and phase as necessary.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">317.2.</div><div class="rule-text">End of Turn Cleanup</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Invoke an End of Turn Special Cleanup. See rule 318. Cleanups for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Insert &quot;2c. Heal all Units .&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">317.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Expiration Step</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">All &quot;this turn&quot; effects expire simultaneously.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">317.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">As the Expiration Step ends, all players&#x27; Rune Pools empty. Any unspent Energy and Power are lost.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">317.4.</div><div class="rule-text">The Turn Player then becomes the next player in Turn Order.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">318.</div><div class="rule-text">Cleanups</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">319.</div><div class="rule-text">A Cleanup occurs at the following times:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.1.</div><div class="rule-text">After the game transitions to or from an Open or Closed state</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.2.</div><div class="rule-text">After the game transitions between Phases</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.3.</div><div class="rule-text">After a Pending Item becomes a Legal Item on the Chain</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.4.</div><div class="rule-text">After a Chain Item is removed from the Chain for any reason</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.5.</div><div class="rule-text">After any number of Game Objects enter or leave the Board</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.6.</div><div class="rule-text">After the status of any number of Game Objects changes for any reason</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">319.7.</div><div class="rule-text">After a Move is completed</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">320.</div><div class="rule-text">While a Cleanup is occurring, Chain Items cannot be Resolved.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">320.1.</div><div class="rule-text">New Pending Items can be added, but Legal Items cannot be executed and Priority and Focus are not passed or awarded.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">321.</div><div class="rule-text">If an event occurs during a Cleanup that qualifies for a Cleanup, another Cleanup will occur immediately after the first completes, repeating until a Cleanup occurs with no new change in the game&#x27;s state.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">322.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Cleanup occurs, the following steps occur in order:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.1.</div><div class="rule-text">1. If a player has as many points as the Victory Score , that player wins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">322.</div><div class="rule-text">2 2. Handle outstanding board state</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">322.</div><div class="rule-text">3 2a. All Units that have non-zero Damage marked on them equalling or exceeding their Might that have Deathknell abilities will trigger their Deathknell ability now, making note of their current location, attributes, and other information relevant to add the trigger as a Pending Item See rule 734 Deathknell for more information .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.4.</div><div class="rule-text">2b. All Units that have non-zero Damage marked on them equalling or exceeding their Might are killed and placed in their owners&#x27; Trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.5.</div><div class="rule-text">3. Assign or Remove the Attacker or Defender designation from Units as needed if there is a Combat in progress</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">322.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are Units present at the Battlefield the Combat is taking place at, but do not have a designation, they gain the same designation as their Controller now</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">322.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are Units present at the Battlefield the Combat is taking place at, but have the opposite designation of their controller, they lose that designation, and gain the same designation as their controller now</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">322.5.c.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are Units at locations other than the Battlefield that the Combat is taking place at, but have either Attacker or Defender designations, they lose those designations now</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.6.</div><div class="rule-text">4. Battlefields with no Units occupying them and no Contested status become Uncontrolled.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.7.</div><div class="rule-text">5. Recall all Gear at Battlefields. Remove all Hidden cards from all Battlefields that are not controlled by the same player and place them in their owner&#x27;s Trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.8.</div><div class="rule-text">6. Mark a Showdown as Staged at each Battlefield that Contested was applied to that is Uncontrolled .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.8.</div><div class="rule-text">a The Showdown remains Staged at each Battlefield that is Contested and has only units present controlled by the player that applied Contested</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">322.</div><div class="rule-text">9 6a. If Units of an opposing player are present at a Battlefield that has a Showdown staged before it can be Opened, the Showdown will cease being Staged</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.10.</div><div class="rule-text">7. Mark a Combat as Staged at each Battlefield that Contested was applied to that have Units present controlled by opposing players.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">322.10.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The Combat remains Staged at that Battlefield as long as there are Units present from two opposing players there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">322.</div><div class="rule-text">11 7a. If Units of two opposing players are no longer present at a Battlefield that has a Combat Staged before it has opened, the Combat will cease being Staged</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.12.</div><div class="rule-text">8. Finalize any Pending Items on the Chain</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.13.</div><div class="rule-text">9. If the current state is a Neutral Open State and one or more Showdowns are Staged , the Turn Player chooses one of those Battlefields. A Showdown begins there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">322.14.</div><div class="rule-text">10. If the current state is a Neutral Open State and Combat is Staged at one or more Battlefields , the Turn Player chooses one of those Battlefields . Combat begins there.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">323.</div><div class="rule-text">Special Cleanups are Cleanup steps invoked at specific times that have additional steps not present in a normal Cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Special Cleanup is invoked, the unique steps added will be inserted and defined by the sub-section that invokes it. Example: When a Combat Cleanup is invoked, the Combat section defines what steps are added to the Cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">323.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If events during a Special Cleanup require another Cleanup, a normal Cleanup is invoked, not another iteration of the Special Cleanup .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">324.</div><div class="rule-text">Chains and Showdowns</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">325.</div><div class="rule-text">Players can act during the following Windows of Opportunity that occur during the course of regular play:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">325.1.</div><div class="rule-text">During a Chain</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">325.2.</div><div class="rule-text">During a Showdown</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">326.</div><div class="rule-text">Chains</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">327.</div><div class="rule-text">The Chain is a Non-Board Zone that temporarily exists whenever a card is played or an ability is activated.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">327.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards are placed here as part of the process of being played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">327.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Abilities are queued here as part of the process of resolving. See rule 357. Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">328.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards and abilities added to the chain are added as Pending Chain Items that become Finalized Chain Items.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">328.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Pending Items are on the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">328.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Chain Items are Pending until the &quot;Check Legality&quot; step of playing a card. See rule 346. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">328.3.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Pending Chain Item is no longer Pending it is finalized and becomes a Finalized Chain Item .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">329.</div><div class="rule-text">The Chain exists as long as a Chain Item is on it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">329.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Only one Chain can exist at a time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">329.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If a card would begin to be played while a Chain already exists, it is placed on the existing Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">330.</div><div class="rule-text">The State of the Turn is partially determined by whether or not the Chain currently exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">330.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The turn is said to be in a Closed State if a Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">330.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards of all Categories, by default, cannot be played during a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">330.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Card abilities, by default, cannot be played during a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">330.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The turn is said to be in an Open State if no Chain exists.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">331.</div><div class="rule-text">Steps of Resolving Chain Items</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">332.</div><div class="rule-text">Whenever a card or token is played or an ability is activated or triggered, a Chain is created.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">332.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The player that created the chain becomes the first Active Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">332.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The Active Player is a designator similar to, but distinct from, Turn Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">332.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Similar to the Turn Player , this designation will pass between players over the course of play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">333.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 1: Finalize</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">333.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If one or more Items are Pending , their controllers must complete the steps of Playing those Pending Items until they are Finalized Items or leave the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">333.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This process does not pass Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">333.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Item is Finalized in the order it was appended to the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">333.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Abilities that Add resources, Units , and Gear resolve immediately when Finalized and do not progress to Step 2: Execute. See rule 346. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">333.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is empty, play proceeds in an Open State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">333.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is not empty and there are one or more Pending Items , repeat Step 1.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">333.1.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is not empty and there are no Pending Items , the controller of the newest item on the chain gains Priority and becomes the Active Player. Proceed to Step 2: Execute.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">334.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 2: Execute</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">334.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Active Player may do any the following:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">334.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Play a Card that is legally timed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards , by default, cannot be played during a Closed State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A Legally Timed Card would be a Card with Reaction.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.a.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Other exceptions may be created during regular play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.a.4.</div><div class="rule-text">The card will be added to the chain as a Pending Item , following the steps of playing a card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.a.5.</div><div class="rule-text">This can be an additional card to the item that Started the Chain in the case of the first Active Player after creating the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.a.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Whether a Card is legally timed is evaluated during the &quot;Check Legality&quot; step of Playing a Card. See rule 346. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.a.7.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing a card will create one or more Pending Items . Return to Step 1: Finalize.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">334.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Activate Abilities of Game Objects that are legally timed. See rule 386. Playing or Activating Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">All rules for legally timed cards apply to legally timed abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Activating abilities will create one or more Pending Items . Return to Step 1: Finalize.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">334.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Pass Priority</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">334.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Active Player passes Priority to the next Player in Turn Order. Proceed to Step 3: Pass.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">335.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 3: Pass</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">335.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If all players have passed Priority without adding any items to the Chain , proceed to Step 4: Resolve.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">335.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Otherwise, the Active Player passes Priority to the next Player in Turn Order. Return to Step 3: Execute.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">336.</div><div class="rule-text">Step 4: Resolve</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">336.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The newest item on the Chain resolves. Execute its game effects in their entirety. See rule 346. Playing Cards for more information on resolving spells. See rule 386. Playing or Activating Abilities for more information on resolving abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">336.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is empty, play proceeds in an Open State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">336.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is not empty and there are one or more Pending Items , return to Step 1: Finalize.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">336.4.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Chain is not empty and there are no Pending Items , the controller of the newest item on the chain gains Priority and becomes the Active Player. Return to Step 2: Execute.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">337.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdowns</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">338.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown is a Window of Opportunity in which Players have an Open State in which they may play Spells in an alternating fashion.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">338.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Each spell played this way creates a Chain as normal.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">339.</div><div class="rule-text">The State of the turn is partially determined by whether or not a Showdown is in progress.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">339.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The turn is said to be in a Showdown State if a Showdown is in progress.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">339.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards of all Categories, by default, cannot be played during a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">339.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Card abilities, by default, cannot be played during a Showdown State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">339.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The turn is said to be in a Neutral State if no Showdown is in progress.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">340.</div><div class="rule-text">A Showdown begins when Control of a Battlefield is Contested and the turn is in a Neutral Open State.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">340.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If Control of a Battlefield is Contested between two players, then a Showdown will be opened as the first step of Combat. See rule 437. Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">340.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If Control of a Battlefield is Contested and the Battlefield in question is uncontrolled when it becomes Contested , a Showdown is opened during the Cleanup at the end of the action that caused the Battlefield to become Contested.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">341.</div><div class="rule-text">As a Showdown begins, the player who applied Contested status to the Battlefield gains Focus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">342.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Showdown begins, it may or may not begin with an Initial Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">342.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Showdowns that open as a result of Combat may have an Initial Chain of Triggered Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">342.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">These Triggered Abilities should be put on the chain first by the player with Focus , then proceeding with players without the Defender designation in Turn Order. Finally, the player with the Defender designation will add their Triggered Abilities , if any, to the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">342.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If there are no such Triggered Abilities present during a Combat -initiated Showdown then no Initial Chain is created, but the Showdown will still proceed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">343.</div><div class="rule-text">When the last item on the chain resolves during a Showdown , Focus passes, and the next Player gains both Focus and Priority.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">343.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Focus does not pass when the last item on the Initial Chain resolves, if there was one. Instead the player with Focus proceeds with play.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">344.</div><div class="rule-text">During a Showdown , the player with Focus may do one of the following:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">344.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Play a spell that is legally timed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">344.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The spell will start a Chain as normal.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">344.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Activate Abilities of Game Objects that are legally timed. See rule 357. Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">344.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Pass.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">344.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If all Players have passed once in sequence, the Showdown ends.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">344.3.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Perform a Cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">344.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Otherwise, Focus passes to the next Player in Turn Order.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">345.</div><div class="rule-text">If all players pass Focus without playing a spell or activating an ability, then the Showdown Closes.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">345.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If this Showdown opened as a result of Combat, proceed with the remaining steps of Combat to resolve the phase. See rule 441. The Steps of Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">345.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If this Showdown opened as a result of Contested being applied to a Battlefield without a controller, do one of the following:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">345.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If only one player&#x27;s Units remain at the Battlefield , and if that player does not already Control the Battlefield , that player establishes Control over the Battlefield . See rule 179. Control for more information on Control . See rule 446.1. for more information on Conquering .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">345.2.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This results in a Conquer if that player has not yet scored that Battlefield this turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">345.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If two players&#x27; Units remain at the Battlefield , Control cannot be established and the Battlefield remains Contested . This results in a Staged Combat . See rule 437. Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">345.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The player who applied Contested to the Battlefield will be the Attacker in the subsequent Combat.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">346.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing Cards</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">347.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing a card is the act of a player utilizing their cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">347.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A card is Played when it has finished this process in its entirety.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">347.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Tokens are not cards, but can still be Played. See rule 173. Tokens for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">348.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards have different behaviors when played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">348.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Permanents become Game Objects when Played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">348.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Spells create game effects that are executed, then the card is placed in the trash when Played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">349.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards have different states during the process of being played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">349.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When initially being played cards are Pending, as Pending Chain Items.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">349.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Near the end of the process cards will cease being Pending and become Finalized Chain Items .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">350.</div><div class="rule-text">The Process of Play</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">351.</div><div class="rule-text">1. Remove the card from the zone you are playing it from and put it onto the Chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">351.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This Closes the State. See rule 307. States of the Turn for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">351.2.</div><div class="rule-text">This item becomes Pending.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">351.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If another Card Effect or ability is currently resolving, continue resolving it before proceeding with any further steps of this process.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">352.</div><div class="rule-text">2. Make necessary choices.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the card is a spell, or has an effect that specifies a choice &quot;As I am played,&quot; those choices are made now.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.2.</div><div class="rule-text">For Units , choose a valid Location where that Unit will be placed upon being Played.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.2.</div><div class="rule-text">a By default, Valid locations include the controller&#x27;s Base or a Battlefield the controller controls.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.2.</div><div class="rule-text">b Some Game Effects may grant players permission to play Units to locations that are not normally Valid . Such locations become Valid for the purposes of Playing the Unit. .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.3.</div><div class="rule-text">For Spells and Abilities that Move one or more Units , choose a valid Location as the Move Destination for each Move that will be performed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.4.</div><div class="rule-text">If a card requires you to specifically choose one or more Game Objects , that choice is made now.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This does not include cards that affect one or more Game Objects based on criteria. Example: &quot;Stun a unit at a battlefield&quot; is a Choice. Example: &quot;Kill all gear&quot; is not a Choice.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">This does not include making choices for Triggered Abilities of permanents, even if those abilities trigger when the permanent is played. Example: A unit with a triggered ability that says &quot;When I&#x27;m played, kill a unit&quot; does not require you to choose a target as it&#x27;s played. The target will be chosen when the ability triggers. See rule 375. Triggered Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Targeting</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.6.</div><div class="rule-text">When a card Chooses one or more specific Game Objects to affect, it is Targeted.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.7.</div><div class="rule-text">In order to put a spell or ability on the chain, valid choices must be made for all targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.8.</div><div class="rule-text">A target is a valid choice if it meets all of the following requirements:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.8.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is a permanent or rune on the board, a spell or ability on the chain, a player or zone, or specified explicitly or implicitly as being in some other zone. e.g., &quot;Kill a unit&quot; targets a unit on the board. e.g., &quot;Recycle a unit from your trash&quot; targets a unit card in your trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">352.8.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">&quot;Unit,&quot; &quot;gear,&quot; and &quot;rune&quot; refer to objects on the Board unless specified otherwise.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">352.8.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">&quot;Spell&quot; and &quot;ability&quot; refer to objects on the Chain unless specified otherwise.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">352.8.a.3.</div><div class="rule-text">&quot;Facedown card&quot; refers to a card in a Facedown Zone unless specified otherwise.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">352.8.a.4.</div><div class="rule-text">&quot;Legend&quot; refers to a legend in the Legend Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">352.8.a.5.</div><div class="rule-text">&quot;Chosen Champion&quot; and &quot;unit in the Champion Zone&quot; refer to a unit in the Champion Zone unless specified otherwise.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.8.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It meets all targeting restrictions. e.g., A unit is a valid target for a spell that refers to a &quot;unit at a battlefield,&quot; &quot;enemy unit,&quot; &quot;unit you control,&quot; or &quot;unit with Might 4 or greater&quot; only if it meets the appropriate criteria.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.8.c.</div><div class="rule-text">It is not the spell or ability itself. e.g., A spell that says &quot;Counter a spell&quot; cannot target itself. e.g., An ability of a permanent can target that permanent, because abilities and their sources are separate objects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.9.</div><div class="rule-text">If a spell or ability requires one or more players to choose objects, players, or zones that are not targets, those choices are made on resolution.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.9.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Passive abilities never have targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.9.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Replacement effects never have targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.9.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Units and gear never have targets, although their abilities may.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.10.</div><div class="rule-text">A game object, player, or zone mentioned in the text of a spell, activated ability, or triggered ability is a target UNLESS any of the following are true:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.10.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is in a zone whose information status is not Public. e.g., &quot;Ready a legend&quot; targets a legend, because the Legend Zone is Public. e.g., &quot;Return a unit from your trash to your hand&quot; targets a unit card in your trash, because your trash is Public. e.g., &quot;You may play a unit from your hand, ignoring its costs&quot; does not target a unit card in your hand, because your hand is not a public zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">352.10.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Public zones are Battlefield Zones, Bases, Trashes, Legend Zones, Champion Zones, and Facedown Zones.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.10.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It is included only as part of a targeting restriction for another choice. e.g., &quot;Kill a unit at a battlefield&quot; targets a unit, but not a battlefield, because the units are targets and &quot;at a battlefield&quot; is a restriction. e.g., &quot;Kill all units at a battlefield&quot; targets a battlefield, but not any units. e.g., &quot;Move a unit to a battlefield&quot; targets both a unit and a battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.10.c.</div><div class="rule-text">It is included only as part of a cost, trigger condition, or replacement effect. e.g., &quot;As an additional cost to play me, kill a friendly unit&quot; doesn&#x27;t target anything. e.g., &quot;When a friendly unit dies, kill a gear&quot; targets a gear, but not a friendly unit. e.g., &quot;When you play me, the next time a friendly unit would die this turn, return it to your hand instead&quot; doesn&#x27;t target anything. The replacement effect applies when any friendly unit dies. e.g., &quot;Choose a friendly unit. The next time it would die this turn, return it to your hand instead&quot; targets a friendly unit, because &quot;choose a friendly unit&quot; is not part of the replacement effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">352.10.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This includes costs within instructions, identified by phrases like &quot;[do X] to [do Y].&quot; The cost within that instruction is &quot;[do X].&quot; e.g., &quot;When I hold, you may kill another friendly unit here to draw 1&quot; does not target anything. e.g., &quot;When you play me, you may spend a buff to move a friendly unit&quot; targets the friendly unit, but not the buff.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.10.d.</div><div class="rule-text">It is programmatically selected based on its characteristics rather than chosen by the spell or ability&#x27;s controller. e.g., &quot;Kill all units at a battlefield&quot; targets a battlefield, but does not target any units. e.g., &quot;Kill all units at battlefields&quot; doesn&#x27;t target anything. e.g., &quot;Destroy a unit. Its controller draws 2 cards&quot; targets the unit, but not its controller. e.g., &quot;Ready your legend&quot; doesn&#x27;t target anything, because you can only have one legend. e.g., &quot;Ready a friendly legend&quot; targets a legend, because in a 2v2 game there are two friendly legends. e.g., &quot;Recycle all cards in your trash&quot; doesn&#x27;t target anything, because it affects all cards and you only have one trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">352.10.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">This exception applies solely to objects for which no choice is ever possible.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">352.10.d.2.</div><div class="rule-text">This exception does not apply to objects that are the only valid choice at the moment a spell or ability is placed on the chain, but which would require a choice under other circumstances. e.g., &quot;Kill a unit at a battlefield&quot; always targets a unit, even if that unit is the only unit currently at a battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.10.e.</div><div class="rule-text">It is part of a set of objects chosen in whole or in part by other players. e.g., &quot;Each player kills a unit they control&quot; does not target. Each player, including the one who played the spell, chooses a unit to kill as the spell or ability resolves.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.10.f.</div><div class="rule-text">It is identified in an instruction that a player &quot;must&quot; complete. e.g., &quot;You must recycle one of your runes&quot; doesn&#x27;t target anything. You choose from among your runes as the spell or ability resolves. e.g., &quot;Recycle a rune you control&quot; targets a rune. You choose a rune you control as you put the spell or ability on the chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.11.</div><div class="rule-text">Some cards identify a group of Targets with Targeting Requirements that must be met by the group as a whole.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.11.a.</div><div class="rule-text">As they&#x27;re finalized on the chain, such cards can choose any group of valid targets that collectively fulfill the targeting restriction.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.11.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If the group of targets no longer collectively fulfill the targeting restriction as the spell or ability resolves, that spell or ability&#x27;s controller can choose a subset of the original targets that fulfills the targeting requirement for the spell or ability to affect. Example: A player plays Fox-Fire, a spell that says in part &quot;Kill any number of units at a battlefield with total Might 4 or less.&quot; That player chooses four 1 [M] Recruit tokens at a single battlefield. As a Reaction, another player gives two of those Recruits +1 [M], so the Recruits&#x27; Mights are 1, 1, 2, and 2. Then Fox-Fire resolves. The Recruits no longer have total Might 4 or less, so Fox-Fire&#x27;s controller must choose a legal subset of the original targets to affect. They could choose to kill the two 2 [M] Recruits, or the two 1 [M] Recruits plus one 2 [M] Recruit. The units they choose are Fox-Fire&#x27;s remaining legal targets. They can&#x27;t choose to affect units at the same battlefield that weren&#x27;t initially chosen as targets, and they can&#x27;t affect any units that are no longer at the chosen battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.12.</div><div class="rule-text">If a card specifies that a player may choose some number of Game Objects to be affected by a card, then all choices are considered targeted and chosen independently.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.13.</div><div class="rule-text">If a card specifies that a player chooses &quot;any number&quot; or &quot;up to&quot; some number of Game Objects to be affected, they may choose any number of available targets, including zero. If they choose zero, the spell or ability can be played without any targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.14.</div><div class="rule-text">Splitting</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.14.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If a card specifies that an amount of damage may be split among some number of Units , then each Unit chosen is Targeted.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.14.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The Targets are chosen when the spell or ability is finalized on the chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.14.c.</div><div class="rule-text">A number of Targets can only be chosen up to, and not exceeding, the initial amount of damage available when the spell is played. Example: A player playing a spell that instructs them to &quot;Split 5 damage&quot; may only choose up to 5 units, but may choose fewer.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.14.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Target is valid, and contributes to Chosen triggers individually.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.14.e.</div><div class="rule-text">The choice of how much damage is divided across the split is not decided until the resolution of the spell or ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.14.f.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Target must receive a valid amount of damage.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.14.g.</div><div class="rule-text">Valid damage is a positive integer amount, greater than or equal to 1 damage.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.14.h.</div><div class="rule-text">If, at resolution of the spell or effect, there are more Targets than available damage to divide, then the player who controls the effect dealing damage determines which Targets cease being Targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">352.14.i.</div><div class="rule-text">Any costs that were paid, or effects that were triggered as a result of those Game Objects being chosen as Targets remain in effect, paid, or otherwise triggered.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">352.15.</div><div class="rule-text">These choices cannot be changed after this step.</div></div>
