<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">465.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Format: Best of 1. The first player to reach the Victory Score in Points wins the Match.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">465.7.</div><div class="rule-text">First Turn Process: The player going first does not draw a card during their first Draw Phase of the game. The player going last channels an extra Rune from their Rune Deck during their first Channel Phase of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">466.</div><div class="rule-text">2v2 (Magma Chamber)</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.1.</div><div class="rule-text">4 Players</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.2.</div><div class="rule-text">2v2 2 opponents each 1 teammate</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Victory Score: 11</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefield Count: 3</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player provides one (1) Battlefield , included in their deck during deck building.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">The player who is taking the first turn removes their Battlefields. They will not be used.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Setup:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Each player who is not going first randomly selects one (1) of their three (3) Battlefields . The other two are removed and will not be used for this game. The selected Battlefields are placed between the players before play and will be used for this game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Turn order alternates teams.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.5.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The first player will be followed by an opponent, then the first player&#x27;s teammate, then the first opponent&#x27;s teammate, and so on.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.5.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If allies are sitting across from each other, turn order proceeds clockwise as normal.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.5.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If allies are sitting next to each other, turn order is passed across the table.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Format: Best of 1. The first team to reach the Victory Score in Points wins the Match.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Teammates win or lose together.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.6.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If one player Concedes , then the entire team loses.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.6.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If one player Loses, then the entire team loses.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.6.a.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If one player Wins , then the entire team wins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.7.</div><div class="rule-text">First Turn Process: The player going first does not draw a card during their first Draw Phase of the game. The player going last channels an extra Rune from their Rune Deck during their first Channel Phase of the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-1"><div class="rule-id">466.8.</div><div class="rule-text">Unique Rules</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.8.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Players may play spells during their Teammate&#x27;s Turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.8.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Battlefields controlled during the Beginning Phase of a player&#x27;s turn by that player&#x27;s teammate are disqualified from being scored by that Team, that turn. Example: A player may not induce their partner to retreat, and then conquer a Battlefield their teammate was controlling.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.8.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Control is not shared.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.8.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Players may not Hide cards at Battlefields controlled by their Teammate.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.8.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Players may not issue Standard Movement to their Teammate&#x27;s Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.8.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Friendly describes controlled Game Objects by a player or their Teammate. Example: &quot;When I am played, ready a friendly unit &quot; could target a player&#x27;s own Units or their teammate&#x27;s Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.8.e.</div><div class="rule-text">Hands are still Private Information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.8.e.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Players are not restricted in what they say to their Teammate, however.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">466.8.e.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Feel free to openly communicate, honestly or cryptically.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-4"><div class="rule-id">466.8.e.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Revealing Cards is still a game action and cannot be done unless instructed. See rule 411. Reveal for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.8.f.</div><div class="rule-text">The Final Point has an adjustment to the criteria when scoring.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.8.f.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When scoring the Final Point from Conquer , a player must Score each Battlefield in the same turn, excepting any that were occupied by their ally during that turn&#x27;s Beginning Phase .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">466.8.f.2.</div><div class="rule-text">No other changes to Final Point restrictions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.8.g.</div><div class="rule-text">Teammates may not utilize the same Champion Legend .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">466.8.h.</div><div class="rule-text">Teammates may not utilize the same Battlefields .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">649.</div><div class="rule-text">Conceding</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">650.</div><div class="rule-text">A player may concede at any time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">651.</div><div class="rule-text">When a player concedes, they are removed from the game in progress.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">651.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If only one other player is remaining after a player has conceded, the player remaining Wins.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">651.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If more than one player remains after a concession, follow the steps for the Removal of a Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">651.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Removal of a player involves them no longer being able to make choices or otherwise influence the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">651.4.</div><div class="rule-text">If the player has Teammates due to the Mode of Play , that player&#x27;s Teammates also lose and are removed from the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">652.</div><div class="rule-text">If the game continues, follow these steps for Removal of a Player.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Banish all permanents and runes they currently control and all permanents and runes they own.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Remove the Battlefield they contributed to the game if it is in use.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If it was in use, replace it with a token battlefield with no abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Any units or hidden cards there do not move and are otherwise unaffected by this process.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.2.c.</div><div class="rule-text">If the removed battlefield was applying any continuous effects, those continuous effects immediately cease, which may cause changes in the characteristics of units or hidden cards there. Example: A battlefield reads &quot;Units here have +1 [M].&quot; If that battlefield&#x27;s owner concedes and the battlefield is removed from the game as a result, units there immediately cease to get +1 [M].</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Remove all cards they own from the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Counter all spells and abilities of all types controlled by the player that has conceded.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">652.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Proceed with the game.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Turn</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the removed player was the Turn Player , play proceeds in Turn Order to the next available player in order.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Focus</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the removed player had Focus in a Showdown , the next Player in order receives Focus .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the player being removed creates a state where all Players have Passed their Focus , the Showdown ends and play proceeds as necessary, E.G. Combat is resolved or a Cleanup is completed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">652.5.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Priority</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the removed player had Priority during a Chain , the next Player in order receives Priority .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">652.5.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the player being removed creates a state where all Players have passed Priority , then the most recent spell or ability on the Chain will resolve with Priority being re-established as appropriate for the state after the resolution of that spell or ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-chapter level-0"><div class="rule-id">700.</div><div class="rule-text">Additional Rules</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">701.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">702.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs are objects placed on Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">702.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs can be tracked with a buff reminder card from a Riftbound booster pack or with any spare object in your surroundings.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">702.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs can be added or spent.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">702.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">To Buff a Unit , a player chooses a Unit and then places a buff on it. That Unit is Buffed for as long as the buff remains on it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">702.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Spending a Buff removes a single Buff counter from a Unit .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">702.2.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A buff cannot be spent from a Unit that does not have a buff.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">702.2.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">A player can only spend buffs on units they control.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">702.3.</div><div class="rule-text">There can only be one Buff on a Unit at a time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">702.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Buff is added, or instructed to be added, on a Unit that already has a Buff , it is not placed instead.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">703.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Buff individually contributes +1 Might to a Unit.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">704.</div><div class="rule-text">Buffs are Game Objects and may be referenced, counted, or targeted by other effects as specified.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">705.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Unit leaves play, remove all Buffs from it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">705.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Champions do not retain Buffs in the Champion Zone, even if they return there somehow.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">706.</div><div class="rule-text">Mighty</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">707.</div><div class="rule-text">Mighty is a description that applies to some units. Other game effects can check whether a unit is Mighty.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">708.</div><div class="rule-text">A Unit &quot;is Mighty&quot; as long as its Might is 5 or greater.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">709.</div><div class="rule-text">A Unit &quot;becomes Mighty&quot; at the moment its Might changes from being less than 5 to being 5 or greater. Example: A Unit with Might 4 that gets +1 [M] becomes Mighty . Example: A Unit with Might 5 that gets +1 [M] does not become Mighty , because it was already Mighty.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">710.</div><div class="rule-text">Units on the board are evaluated according to their current Might. Example: A unit with a base Might of 3 is targeted by a spell that reads &quot;A unit gets +3 [M] this turn.&quot; As that spell resolves, its Might changes from 3 to 6, and it becomes Mighty . When that effect expires at the end of the turn, it will no longer be Mighty.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">711.</div><div class="rule-text">Units in Non-Board Zones are evaluated according to their inherent Might. Example: A unit in the trash is Mighty if its printed Might is 5 or greater. It doesn&#x27;t matter if there were effects raising or lowering its might while it was on the board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">712.</div><div class="rule-text">Bonus Damage</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">713.</div><div class="rule-text">Bonus Damage is an intrinsic property that can be granted to Deal actions that influence the amount of Damage that the action is distributing.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">714.</div><div class="rule-text">If more than one instance of Bonus Damage is applied or granted to a Deal action, all instances are summed and applied once.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">714.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Bonus Damage can only be a positive value, and can only increase the amount of Damage being distributed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">714.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If, for any reason, Bonus Damage would be a negative number, then no Bonus Damage is applied to the action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">715.</div><div class="rule-text">Bonus Damage applies to the total damage Dealt by one instance of the action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">715.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Deal action has a single target, the amount of Damage to that target will be increased by the Bonus Damage granted to it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">715.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Deal action has multiple targets, the amount of Damage dealt to each target is increased by Bonus Damage individually and separately. Example: Singularity is a spell that says &quot;Deal 6 to each of up to two units.&quot; A player plays Singularity while they also control Annie, Fiery, a unit that says &quot;Your spells and abilities deal 1 Bonus Damage.&quot; Singularity deals 1 Bonus Damage to both of its targets, dealing 7 to each.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">715.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Deal action Splits damage, then the Bonus Damage applies to the amount of Damage that will be Split . This can alter the number of targets eligible to be chosen. Example: Volibear, Furious is a unit that says in part &quot;When I attack, deal 5 damage split among any number of enemy units here.&quot; A player attacks with Volibear, Furious while they also control Annie, Fiery, a unit that says &quot;Your spells and abilities deal 1 Bonus Damage.&quot; Volibear, Furious now deals 6 damage split among any number of enemy units at its location, and can choose to split that damage among up to 6 units rather than the usual 5.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">716.</div><div class="rule-text">Attachment</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">717.</div><div class="rule-text">Attaching is a limited action that causes cards to become linked to each other to combine their effects in some way. This causes one card to become Attached and the other to become A Top-Most Card. See rule 421 Attach for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">718.</div><div class="rule-text">Attached is the state of a card being linked to another card in this way.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">718.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A card remains in this state until Detached.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">718.2.</div><div class="rule-text">While in this state, the card&#x27;s Rules Text is Inactive. See rule 720 Inactive for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">718.3.</div><div class="rule-text">While in this state, Abilities in the card&#x27;s Effect Text are appended to the Rules Text of the Top-Most Card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">718.4.</div><div class="rule-text">While in this state, the card&#x27;s Might Bonus modulates the Top-Most Card &#x27;s Might by the value listed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">718.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Attached cards still have all properties of being a card on the board while in this state.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">718.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Attached cards still have all Types and Tags while Attached.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">718.5.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Attached cards still can be chosen or targeted by game effects while Attached.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">718.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Attached cards cannot be moved separately from the Top-Most Card they are Attached to.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">718.7.</div><div class="rule-text">A card may be Attached only to a single Top-Most card at a time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">718.8.</div><div class="rule-text">Attached cards may have different Controllers from their Top-Most card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">718.8.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Changes in Control of the Top-Most card do not impact Control of Attached cards and vice versa.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">718.8.b.</div><div class="rule-text">An Attached card still appends the abilities in its Effect Text to the Rules Text of the Top-Most card and modulates the Top-Most Card &#x27;s Might by its Might Bonus.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">719.</div><div class="rule-text">A Top-Most Card is a card that has one or more cards linked to it through the process of Attaching.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">719.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Effect Text of all cards Attached to this card are appended to the Rules Text of this card for as long as they remain Attached.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">719.2.</div><div class="rule-text">This card ceases being a Top-Most Card when there are no longer any cards Attached to it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">719.3.</div><div class="rule-text">A Top-Most Card and all cards Attached to it are at the same location.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">719.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">When the Top-Most Card moves, all Attached cards move with it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">719.4.</div><div class="rule-text">The Exhausted and Ready state of the Top-Most card does not affect nor change the status of the Attached cards and vice versa.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">719.5.</div><div class="rule-text">When a Top-Most Card changes zones from a board zone to a non-board zone, all Attached cards Detach from it, remaining in their current zones.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">719.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The player that controls the Top-Most Card that changed zones decides the order these cards Detach in, and thus the order of any relevant effects that occur due to the Detach occurring.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">720.</div><div class="rule-text">Inactive</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">721.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Card text can occasionally be assigned to be ignored, disregarded, or otherwise rendered as not applicable during the course of play. This state is referred to as Inactive.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">721.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Text marked this way is not applied at all while in this state.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">721.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Inactive Abilities do not trigger, do not apply, and cannot be activated. Inactive instructions are not processed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">722.</div><div class="rule-text">Inactive text is still present on cards.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">722.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards with Inactive text still have keywords for the sake of Game Effects that want to reference or see if a card has a keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">722.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Game Effects that parse or interpret text to determine target eligibility may still parse Inactive text for the sake of eligibility. Example: Spinning Axe is a gear with [Temporary]. While it&#x27;s attached and its rules text is inactive, its [Temporary] ability doesn&#x27;t trigger. However, a spell that reads &quot;Destroy a gear with [Temporary]&quot; could still choose and destroy Spinning Axe.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">723.</div><div class="rule-text">Rules Text is never Inactive by default.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">724.</div><div class="rule-text">Effect Text is Inactive unless the card with the Effect Text is Attached.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">725.</div><div class="rule-text">Inactive text can partially cease to be Inactive under specific circumstances and exceptions.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">725.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If an Attached card has a Passive or Replacement ability that applies during the process of Attaching or a Triggered ability that triggers off of Attaching , that text exists and can be processed as it Attaches.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">725.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If an Attached card has a Passive or Replacement ability that applies during the process of Detaching or a Triggered ability that triggers off of Detaching , that text exists and can be processed as it Detaches.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">725.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If an Attached card has an Equip ability, the Weaponmaster keyword can reference that Equip ability and any abilities that passively modify that Equip ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">726.</div><div class="rule-text">Keywords</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">727.</div><div class="rule-text">A Keyword is a specific term that appears on Cards that acts as a shorthand for a specific game effect, or ability of any variety.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">727.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A Keyword can be an ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">727.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Keywords can be identified by having a colored highlight behind them.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">727.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The color of the highlight has no effect on gameplay.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">727.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Keywords can be referenced or specified by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">727.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Other effects may grant Keywords.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">727.3.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The definition and rules of the specific Keyword will determine the behavior if a Keyword is granted while it is already present.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">727.3.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect that granted the Keyword will specify the duration for which it is granted.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">727.3.a.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If an effect that grants a Keyword does not specify a duration, the duration is as long as that Game Object remains on the Board or in its current Non-Board Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">727.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Other effects may remove Keywords.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">727.3.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The effect that removed the Keyword will specify the duration it is removed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">727.3.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If an effect that removes a Keyword does not specify a duration, the duration is as long as that Game Object remains on the Board or in its current Non-Board Zone.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">728.</div><div class="rule-text">A card can have any number of Keywords.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">729.</div><div class="rule-text">Similar to other rules text, execute any effects of Keywords in the order listed when reading the card from top to bottom of the rules text.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">730.</div><div class="rule-text">Keyword Glossary</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">731.</div><div class="rule-text">Accelerate</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">731.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Accelerate is a Unit ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">731.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Accelerate is functionally short for &quot;As you play me, you may pay [1] and 1 Power as an additional cost. If you do, I enter ready.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">731.1.a.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the unit has a single domain, the Power portion of the Accelerate cost can be paid only with a Power that matches the domain of the unit.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">731.1.a.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If the unit has no domain or more than one domain, the Power portion of the Accelerate cost can be paid with [A] (a Power of any domain).</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">731.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Accelerate is an Optional Additional Cost to be paid as a player plays the unit with the ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">731.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Accelerate costs cannot be paid while the unit is on the board, only as part of the steps of playing a card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">731.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Accelerate has no function while on the board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">731.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Accelerate are redundant.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">731.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Accelerate, and whether or not a unit has Accelerate, is a characteristic of the Unit and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">731.6.</div><div class="rule-text">Accelerate influences the state of the unit entering the Board. It does not enter exhausted and then become ready.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">731.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Accelerate will not interact with, or trigger, abilities that are affected by units becoming ready.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">732.</div><div class="rule-text">Action</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">732.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Action is a Permissive keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">732.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It can be present on Spells , Units , Rune Abilities, Legend Abilities or Permanent Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">732.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Action grants the corresponding card or effect permission to be played or activated during Showdowns, even when it is not the Controlling player&#x27;s turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">732.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Action is functionally short for the following:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">732.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">On Spells and Units: &quot;This can be played during showdowns on any player&#x27;s turn.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">732.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">On Rune, Legend, or Permanent Abilities: &quot;This can be activated during showdowns on any player&#x27;s turn.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">732.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The card or effect with this keyword is not restricted to showdowns. This permission is inclusive of all other timings and options available to the ability as written or by default.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">732.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Action does not alter the function of any instruction of the corresponding card or effect it is on. It is only permission. Example: Playing a Unit with Action still has the inherent restrictions of playing Units without Action. It can only be played to the controlling player&#x27;s base or a battlefield they control.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">732.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Action is a referenceable characteristic.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">732.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Whether or not a Game Object has Action is a characteristic of that Game Object and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">732.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Whether or not a Spell has Action is a characteristic of that Spell and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">732.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Whether or not an Ability has Action is a characteristic of that Ability and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">733.</div><div class="rule-text">Assault</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">733.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Assault is a Passive Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">733.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is present on Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">733.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Assault is formatted as &quot;Assault [X]&quot;.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">733.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The X is referenced in the functional text of the ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">733.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The X is referred to as the Assault Value.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">733.1.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If X is omitted, it is presumed to be 1.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">733.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">It is functionally short for &quot;While I am an attacker, I have +X [M].&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">733.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Being an attacker means the Unit has gained the Attacker designation during Combat. See rule 437. Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">733.1.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Assault remains in effect as long as the Unit maintains the Attacker designation.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">733.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Unit has Assault or has been granted Assault and is granted Assault by an additional source, the Assault Value of all granted Assault keywords is summed. Example: Petty Officer has Assault. It is chosen as the target of Cleave, which says &quot;Give a unit [Assault 3] this turn.&quot; After Cleave resolves, Petty Officer has Assault 4 this turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">733.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Assault, and whether or not a unit has Assault, is a characteristic of the Unit and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">734.</div><div class="rule-text">Deathknell</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">734.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Deathknell is a Triggered Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">734.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is present on Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">734.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It is formatted as &quot;Deathknell - [Effect]&quot;.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">734.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">[Effect] is the rules text for the specific instance of Deathknell. This is referred to as the Deathknell effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">734.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">It is functionally short for &quot;When I die, [Effect].&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">734.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">[Effect] is the rules text of the Deathknell effect.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">734.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">The Trigger for this effect is the Permanent being Killed and sent to the Trash.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">734.1.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If the Permanent with the effect is not sent to the Trash , for example because its &quot;killed&quot; event was replaced with a recall, the Deathknell will not occur.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">734.1.d.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The trigger will be added to the chain as a Pending Item before the card with Deathknell is moved to the trash due to a Kill instruction or a Cleanup.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">734.1.d.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Before the card with Deathknell is moved to the Trash , note its location, its attributes, and any other details related to the effect of its Deathknell to process the trigger after it has been Finalized .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">734.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Each instance of Deathknell a Permanent may have will trigger separately.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">734.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The controller will choose the order to add these Triggers to the chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">734.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Deathknell, and whether or not a permanent has Deathknell, is a characteristic of the permanent and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">735.</div><div class="rule-text">Deflect</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">735.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Deflect is a Passive Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">735.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is present on Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">735.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It is formatted as &quot;Deflect [X]&quot;.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">735.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The X is referenced in the functional text of the ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">735.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The X is referred to as the Deflect Value.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">735.1.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If X is omitted, it is presumed to be 1.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">735.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">It is functionally short for &quot;Spells and abilities an opponent controls that choose me cost an amount of Power equal to [Deflect Value] more to play as an additional cost.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">735.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Power used to pay this cost may always be of any Domain. Example: A Fury spell targets an Order unit with Deflect. The Power used to pay the Deflect cost can be any Domain; it does not need to match the Domain of the spell or the target.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">735.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">It is an effect that imposes a Mandatory Additional Cost on Spells and Abilities that choose the permanent that has this ability. See rule 346. Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">735.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Unit has Deflect, or has been granted Deflect, and is granted Deflect by an additional source, the Deflect Value of all granted Deflect keywords is summed.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">735.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Deflect, and whether or not a permanent has Deflect, is a characteristic of the permanent and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">736.</div><div class="rule-text">Ganking</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">736.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Ganking is a Passive Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">736.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is present on Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">736.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It is functionally short for &quot;I may move to a battlefield from another battlefield.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">736.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">It is a passive ability that adds permissions to the Unit&#x27;s Standard Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">736.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">It does not restrict or remove options from the Unit&#x27;s Standard Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">736.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">It does not have an activation cost.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">736.1.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">It does not give additional abilities or activations of Movement, only new options for the Standard Move.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">736.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Ganking are redundant.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">736.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Ganking, and whether or not a unit has Ganking, is a characteristic of the Unit and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">737.</div><div class="rule-text">Hidden</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">737.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Hidden is a keyword that acts as a prerequisite to perform the Hide Discretionary Action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">737.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is present on Spells, Units, and Gear.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">737.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It is functionally short for &quot;While this card is in your hand or in the Champion Zone on your turn during an Open State, you may pay [A] to hide this facedown at a battlefield you control that doesn&#x27;t already have a facedown card hidden there for as long as you control that battlefield. Beginning on the next turn, this gains [Reaction] and you may play this, ignoring its base cost.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">737.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">It allows the player to take the Discretionary Action Hide .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">737.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Hide is not a subset of Play .</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">737.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Hiding a card does not open a chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">737.1.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing a card from facedown (or &quot;from Hidden&quot;) does open a chain.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">737.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Some choices made while playing a card from Hidden are restricted to the battlefield where it was hidden. A card cannot be played from Hidden if it is a spell with no valid targets under these restrictions. See rule 352.5. Targeting for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">737.1.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">A hidden unit must be played to that battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">737.1.d.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If a hidden spell or a play effect of a hidden permanent chooses any targets, those targets must be chosen from among options at that battlefield, unless the ability explicitly restricts targeting in a way that makes this impossible. Example: Blastcone Fae is a unit with Hidden and &quot;When you play me, give a unit -2 [M] this turn, to a minimum of 1 [M].&quot; Because this is a play effect, its target must be chosen from among units at the same battlefield if Blastcone Fae was played from Hidden. Example: Tideturner is a unit with Hidden and &quot;When you play me, you may choose a unit you control at another location. Move me to its location and it to my original location.&quot; Because its play ability has a targeting restriction that can never be fulfilled by a unit at its battlefield, its target may be chosen freely from among the available options.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">737.1.d.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If a hidden spell or a play effect of a hidden permanent causes you to play a unit, you must choose to play that unit at that battlefield.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">737.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Abilities and instructions of hidden cards other than the choices listed above function as normal. Example: Stand United is a spell that has Hidden and says &quot;Buff a friendly unit. Buffs give an additional +1 might to friendly units this turn.&quot; If it&#x27;s played from Hidden, the first part of its ability must choose a friendly unit at the same battlefield, but the second part of its ability affects all friendly units with buffs, no matter where they are.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">737.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Instead of being hidden, a card with Hidden may be played for its cost as normal, at its normal timing with no restrictions on targeting.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">737.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Hidden are redundant.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">737.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Hidden, and whether or not a card has Hidden, is a characteristic of the card and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">737.5.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This is independent of the state of being facedown.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">737.6.</div><div class="rule-text">A card that is Hidden gains Reaction while facedown, and may be played any time a card with Reaction may be played as a result.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">737.6.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The property is granted to the card in its facedown state, and is not publicly known.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">738.</div><div class="rule-text">Legion</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">738.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Legion is a Conditional Keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">738.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It can be present on Spells, Units, Rune Abilities, Legend Abilities and Permanent Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">738.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It is formatted as &quot;Legion - [Text]&quot;.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">738.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Starting from the Keyword to the end of the clause, the entire statement is the Legion Ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">738.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">On spells and on play effects of permanents, it is functionally short for &quot;If you have played another Main Deck card before this one already this turn, apply [Text].&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">738.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">On other abilities and instructions, it is functionally short for &quot;If you have played a Main Deck card this turn, apply [Text].&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">738.1.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">This is called the Legion condition.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">738.1.c.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Legion&#x27;s conditional can apply to passive abilities, activated abilities, spell instructions, or even abilities active in zones outside of the board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">738.2.</div><div class="rule-text">All instances of Legion on cards a player controls are satisfied by that player playing a single card. Example: One card has three different Legion Abilities. The Legion Text of all three abilities apply as long as one card has been played by the card&#x27;s controller earlier in the same turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">738.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Legion, and whether or not a card has Legion, is a characteristic of the card and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">739.</div><div class="rule-text">Reaction</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">739.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Reaction is a Permissive keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">739.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It can be present on Spells, Units, Rune Abilities, Legend Abilities and Permanent</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">Abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">739.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Reaction grants the corresponding card or effect all abilities and permissions of Action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">739.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Reaction , additionally, is functionally short for the following:</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">739.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">On Spells: &quot;This can be played during Closed States on any player&#x27;s turn.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">739.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">On Units: &quot;This can be played during Closed States on any player&#x27;s turn.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">739.1.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">On Rune, Legend, or Permanent Abilities: &quot;This can be activated during Closed States on any player&#x27;s turn.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">739.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The corresponding card or effect with this keyword is not restricted to Closed States or Showdowns . This permission is inclusive of all other timings and options available to the ability as written, Action&#x27;s permissions, or by default.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">739.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Reaction does not alter the function of any instruction of the Card, Rune, or Effect it is on. It is only Permission.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">739.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Playing Units with Reaction still has the inherent restrictions of playing Units without Reaction. It can only be played to the controlling player&#x27;s base or a battlefield they control.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">739.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Reaction is a referencable characteristic.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">739.4.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Whether or not a Game Object has Reaction is a characteristic of that Game Object and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">739.4.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Whether or not a Spell has Reaction is a characteristic of that Spell and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">739.4.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Whether or not an Ability has Reaction is a characteristic of that Ability and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">740.</div><div class="rule-text">Shield</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">740.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Shield is a Passive Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">740.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is present on Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">740.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Shield is formatted as &quot;Shield [X]&quot;.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">740.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The X is referenced in the functional text of the ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">740.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The X is referred to as the Shield Value.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">740.1.b.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If X is omitted, it is presumed to be 1.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">740.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">It is functionally short for &quot;While I am a defender, I have +X [M].&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">740.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Being a defender means the Unit has gained the Defender designation during Combat. See rule 437. Combat for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">740.1.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Shield remains in effect as long as the Unit maintains the Defender designation.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">740.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If a Unit has Shield, or has been granted Shield, and is granted Shield by an additional source, the Shield Value of all granted Shield keywords is summed. Example: Stalwart Poro has Shield. It is chosen as the target of Block, which says &quot;Give a unit [Shield 3] and [Tank] this turn.&quot; After Block resolves, Stalwart Poro has Shield 4 this turn.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">740.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Shield, and whether or not a unit has Shield, is a characteristic of the Unit and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">741.</div><div class="rule-text">Tank</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">741.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Tank is a Passive Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">741.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is present on Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">741.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It is functionally short for &quot;I must be assigned lethal damage before any other unit with the same controller as me that does not have [Tank] during combat resolution.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">741.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">It alters how players can elect to assign combat damage during combat.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">741.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Players must still assign lethal damage to a unit before moving to the next when assigning their damage.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">741.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If more than one unit with Tank is present with the same controller in Combat, damage may be assigned to any of them. Units without Tank are invalid assignments until all units with Tank have lethal damage assigned to them.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">741.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Tank are redundant.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">741.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Tank, and whether or not a unit has Tank, is a characteristic of the Unit and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">742.</div><div class="rule-text">Temporary</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">742.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Temporary is a Triggered Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">742.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is present on Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">742.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It is functionally short for &quot;At the start of this permanent&#x27;s controller&#x27;s Beginning Phase, before scoring, kill this.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">742.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The Trigger Condition is the controller of the permanent&#x27;s Beginning Phase occurring.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">742.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Temporary are redundant.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">742.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Temporary, and whether or not a permanent has Temporary, is a characteristic of the permanent and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">743.</div><div class="rule-text">Vision</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">743.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Vision is a Triggered Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">743.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">It is present on Permanents.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">743.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">It is functionally short for &quot;When this is played, look at the top card of your Main Deck. You may recycle it.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">743.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The trigger is the permanent entering the Board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">743.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Vision trigger separately.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">743.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The player may choose to recycle or not recycle for each instance of Vision separately.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">743.2.b.</div><div class="rule-text">If the player does not recycle the top card and nothing else happens in between the triggers resolving, each instance of Vision will see the same card.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">743.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Vision, and whether or not a permanent has Vision, is a characteristic of the permanent and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">744.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">744.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip is an Activated Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">744.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip is normally present on Gear with the tag Equipment.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">744.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip has a cost to activate and Attaches the card with Equip to a chosen Unit when the cost is paid.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">744.1.b.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip&#x27;s choice is a Target.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">744.1.b.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The chosen Unit will become the Top-Most Card for the Attach action.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">744.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip is formatted as &quot; Equip [Cost]&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">744.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">If paying costs or making choices for this ability causes triggered abilities to trigger, they will be placed on the chain above this ability in a Pending state. See rule 369 Activated Abilities for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">744.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip is functionally short for &quot;[Cost]: Attach this gear to a unit you control.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">744.1.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip costs may include both resource costs and non-resource costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">744.1.c.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip abilities may also include text that alters the Equip cost. Such text is taken</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-cont level-1"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">into</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">account</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">when</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">determining</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">a</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">card&#x27;s</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">Equip</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">cost</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">for</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">any</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id"></div><div class="rule-text">reason.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">744.1.c.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip abilities may include text that alters the timing or targeting of the Equip ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">744.2.</div><div class="rule-text">When the Attach action completes from this keyword, the Unit that was chosen is considered to have been Equipped by the Gear with this ability.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">744.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">This is an event other Game Effects and Triggered Abilities can reference.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">744.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Equipped is the state of a Top-Most Card being Attached by one or more cards that are Equipment.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">744.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">The state of being Equipped is synchronous with that of the Attached state of the Equipment.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">744.3.b.</div><div class="rule-text">A Top-Most Card is Equipped as long as one or more of its Attached cards are Equipment.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">744.3.c.</div><div class="rule-text">The state of being Equipped corresponds to a Top-Most card having a card with Equip that is Attached to it.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">744.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Equip are equivalent to multiple Activated Abilities and can each be activated separately by paying the corresponding costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">744.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Equip, and whether or not a Gear has Equip, is a characteristic of the Gear and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">744.5.</div><div class="rule-text">Whether or not a Gear has Equip may be referenced even if the Rules Text of the Gear is Inactive. See rule 716 Attachment for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">745.</div><div class="rule-text">Quick-Draw</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">745.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Quick-Draw is a Triggered Ability keyword. It is also a Permissive keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">745.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Quick-Draw is present on Gear with Equip abilities.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">745.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Cards with Quick-Draw have Reaction inherently.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">745.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Quick-Draw allows cards to be played and Attached using Reaction timing.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">745.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Quick-Draw is functionally short for &quot; [Reaction] &quot; and &quot;When you play this, attach it to a Unit you control.&quot; See rule 716 Attachment for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">745.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Quick-Draw do not trigger separately and have no effect beyond the first.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">745.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Quick-Draw has no function while on the board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">745.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Quick-Draw , and whether or not a gear has Quick-Draw , is a characteristic of the Gear and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">746.</div><div class="rule-text">Repeat</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">746.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Repeat is an Optional Additional Cost keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">746.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Repeat is present on Spells.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">746.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Repeat is an optional cost that player may pay to execute the effect of their spells a second time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-2"><div class="rule-id">746.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Repeat is formatted as &quot; Repeat [Cost]&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">746.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">The Cost is an Additional Cost to be paid during the steps of playing the spell.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">746.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">If a spell has more than one instance of Repeat , each Cost may be paid or not paid individually.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">746.1.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Each Repeat Cost can be paid only a single time.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">746.1.d.</div><div class="rule-text">Repeat is functionally short for &quot;You may pay [Cost] as an additional cost as you play this spell. If you do, execute the instructions of this spell one additional time.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">746.1.d.1.</div><div class="rule-text">When the additional cost is paid, the effect of the spell, upon resolution, will be performed an additional time. Example: Desert&#x27;s Call is a spell with [Repeat] [2] and &quot;Play a 2 [S] Sand Soldier unit token.&quot; If its controller pays its Repeat cost as they play it, the card&#x27;s instruction to play a Sand Soldier is executed twice, as though the card says &quot;Play a 2 [S] Sand Soldier unit token. Play a 2 [S] Sand Soldier unit token.&quot;</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">746.2.</div><div class="rule-text">When a spell&#x27;s effect is performed an additional time with Repeat , choices must be made at the usual time during the Make Relevant Choices step of Playing a Card. See rule 346 Playing Cards for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">746.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Choices made for the additional execution do not have to be the same as the choices made for the initial execution. Example: Rocket Barrage is a spell with [Repeat] [4][C] and &quot;Choose one - Deal 4 to a unit in a base. [or] Kill a gear.&quot; If Rocket Barrage&#x27;s controller pays its Repeat cost as they play it, they may choose the same mode or a different one, and if they choose the same mode, may choose the same target or a different one. If they choose &quot;Kill a gear&quot; twice and choose two different gear, they must specify which gear is the first target and which is the second. As the spell resolves, those two gear will be killed in the chosen order.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">746.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Repeat can be paid for separately. The spell&#x27;s instructions will be executed an additional time for each instance of Repeat that is paid for.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">746.3.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Regardless of the number of times a spell&#x27;s instructions are executed with this keyword, the spell is only Played once.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">746.4.</div><div class="rule-text">Repeat , and whether or not a spell has Repeat , is a characteristic of the Spell and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-heading level-0"><div class="rule-id">747.</div><div class="rule-text">Weaponmaster</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">747.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Weaponmaster is a Triggered Ability keyword.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">747.1.a.</div><div class="rule-text">Weaponmaster is present on Units.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">747.1.b.</div><div class="rule-text">Weaponmaster is a Play Effect that chooses an Equipment you control and allows you to pay its Equip cost at a discount, regardless of the usual timing of the Equip ability, to Attach that Equipment to the unit with Weaponmaster.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">747.1.c.</div><div class="rule-text">Weaponmaster is functionally short for: &quot;When you play me, choose a Card you control with the Equipment tag. Necessary portions of its Rules Text are no longer Inactive if they are currently Inactive. Pay the cost of its Equip ability, reduced by [A], to attach it to this unit.&quot; See rule 716 Attachment for more information.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">747.1.c.1.</div><div class="rule-text">Weaponmaster can choose an Equipment whether it has an Equip ability or not.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">747.1.c.2.</div><div class="rule-text">The cost of the Equip ability is determined as though that Equip ability was being activated choosing the unit with the Weaponmaster ability, as modulated by any abilities that alter Equip costs.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">747.1.c.3.</div><div class="rule-text">If the chosen card&#x27;s Equip cost does not contain [A], it can still be paid, but will not be reduced.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">747.1.c.4.</div><div class="rule-text">If the chosen card doesn&#x27;t have an Equip cost, it can&#x27;t be paid.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">747.1.c.5.</div><div class="rule-text">If the chosen card&#x27;s Equip cost can&#x27;t be paid, if it can&#x27;t be detached from its current Top-Most card, or if it can&#x27;t be attached to the unit with the Weaponmaster ability, it stays in its current location, Attached to anything it was already Attached to.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-3"><div class="rule-id">747.1.c.6.</div><div class="rule-text">The Equip ability is not activated this way, and the unit with the Weaponmaster ability is not chosen.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">747.2.</div><div class="rule-text">Multiple instances of Weaponmaster trigger separately, and can choose different targets.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-2"><div class="rule-id">747.2.a.</div><div class="rule-text">If you choose the same target with multiple instances of Weaponmaster , each will resolve separately.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-1"><div class="rule-id">747.3.</div><div class="rule-text">Weaponmaster has no function while on the board.</div></div>

<div class="rule-row rule-plain level-0"><div class="rule-id">747.</div><div class="rule-text">4 Weaponmaster , and whether or not a unit has Weaponmaster , is a characteristic of the Unit and may be checked or referenced by other Game Effects.</div></div>

</div>
